## Station 42: Llyn-by-the-Sea

**Page ID:** 6038
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Llyn-by-the-Sea

**Summary:**
Llyn-by-the-Sea , or simply known as Llyn , is the major southern terminus of the Stepford Main Line . This station is managed by National Rail .

**Full Content:**

Llyn-by-the-Sea Main Entrance Market Place Dome Platform 0 Platforms 1-4 Platforms 5-8 Platforms 9-11 Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform Overview Lounge Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone LYN E Station headcode Dispatching L Yes (2 slots) P0-6 , P7-11 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Llyn District Zone - Platforms 12 (Numbered 0-11) Tracks 12 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Northshore 1.76 miles / 2.83 kilometres Westwyvern 3.78 miles / 6.08 kilometres Westercoast 5.76 miles / 9.27 kilometres Leighton City 8.99 miles / 14.47 kilometres Terminus Preceding depot Following depot Northshore Depot - Llyn-by-the-Sea , or simply known as Llyn , is the major southern terminus of the Stepford Main Line . This station is managed by National Rail . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , Leighton City , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay and Edgemead ; and Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton and Rayleigh Bay . The Llyn-by-the-Sea Rail Operations Centre is located in this station, which controls Zone E. Sneak peeked Llyn-by-the-Sea 17 December - Version 1.4 Llyn-by-the-Sea added to the network as part of the Llyn-by-the-Sea extension, as a major terminus with 7 platforms, serving Stepford Connect and Stepford Express . Introduced a new kind of junction, "Alternating Points", to diverge and spread out trains to reduce load. Llyn-by-the-Sea is now shown in the intro . Platforms increased from 7 to 12; lines entering the station increased from 4 to 6. The Signaller Training Academy room was changed to include Trainee Signaller desks. Additional props such as bins added to the platforms. Added Stepford Connect & Stepford Express services to the Rayleigh Bay branch . New routes: R050 & R087 24 December - Version 2.1 New route: R088 Trivia [ ] Prior to V1.7.2, the inspiration of this station was debatable. Some in the community say it was based on London King's Cross while some smaller arguments include Liverpool Lime Street , London Liverpool Street and other stations. However, the V1.7.2 version of Llyn-by-the-Sea is heavily based on London King's Cross , evident from the entrance, concourse roofs and the platforms. This station was the 5th station to be revealed on the Llyn extension, revealed on 18 October 2019. This station is the southern end of the Stepford Main Line , with the northern end located at Stepford Central . From this station to Starryloch , it is roughly parallel to the Stepford Central - Morganstown - Leighton Stepford Road line. This station has the third highest number of platforms out of all stations on the SCR network , with 12, after Benton (13) and Stepford Central (16). This station was the first in V1.4 to feature a new kind of junction called "Alternating Points", which "switch from straight to diverging with each train to help ease the load and spread out the arrivals at Llyn-by-the-Sea", with more stations planned to incorporate the feature. Then V1.8 saw the widespread introduction of randomised platform allocation, similar to this. However since then, this has been replaced by randomised allocation as trains no longer diverge to the other track. This station is one of nine stations managed by National Rail , the others being Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , Stepford East , St Helens Bridge , Benton , Morganstown , Leighton City , and Stepford Airport Central . This station is based off a Welsh station name. If the name "Llyn" is translated to English, it means "Lake". This was the second station in SCR to have a terminating platform serving more than one operator, until in V1.7.2 it was changed so that Stepford Connect and Stepford Express use separate platforms. Players can walk to the beach from this station. The station's signage before V1.6 (and the large sign outside the station before V1.7.2) said 'Llyn-by-the-sea', using a lowercase ' s '. However, the maps and destination boards display Llyn-by-the-Sea, using an uppercase '''S'''. The speed limit entering into and leaving from this station used to be 15 MPH, among the lowest speed limit in the entire game. However in V1.7.2, the tunnels and tunnel layout changed as a whole, and the speed limits are now 45 MPH throughout the tunnels and into the station itself. In V2.0 , the 15 MPH returned with the introduction of a 15 MPH speed limit at most terminating platforms across the network. If the player's render distance is high enough, they can barely see the Stepford City Zone over the sea. Before V1.4 (and before The Big Update ), this station could be accessed, and per announcements, was just " Llyn ". This station is the farthest station from Stepford Central via rail. A full Stepford Connect service from Stepford Central to Llyn-by-the-Sea would take 45 minutes, which can be done as R024 or for Stepford Express that can take as long as 23 minutes or short as 17 minutes as R077 and R078 respectively, and variations via Morganstown instead of Benton , such as R080 and R081 . This station is considered as a major terminus and has ticket barriers and machines, seats, lounges and some offices. This station is popular for 'flooding' (purposefully making the station/line very busy) as it is considered to be typically quiet. This station is the fourth station to have a Rail Operations Centre, Llyn-by-the-Sea Rail Operations Centre , after Stepford Central , Stepford East (removed in V1.4.1 ) and Benton . The Zone E ( Edgemead to Llyn) signalling desk was moved here from Starryloch as of V1.7.2. As of V1.7.2, the Stepford Express Headquarters is located here. As of V1.7.2, a new Signaller Training Academy room has also been added. It is speculated that it will play a role in Signaller Training 2.0 in the future. There are two offices for Supervisors and Managers here. They are located next to the Signaller Training Academy and Staff Mess Room respectively. However, both offices have no specific room for each department, unlike the offices at Stepford Central . A Staff Mess Room has also been added in V1.7.2. Only players ranked Dispatcher and above are able to enter. There is a siding just outside Platform 0 at this station, where a Class 68 locomotive is parked. No trains can spawn there though, and players have to spawn at Northshore Depot instead. This is one of three stations in SCR to have a Platform 0, the others being Stepford Central and Stepford Airport Central . The layout of this station is based on the King's Cross (pre-uncrossed layout), demonstrated by the flyover as well as the change of the lines from a DS, DF, UF, US configuration to a DS, US, DF, UF configuration. With the new track layout, there are more platforms for Stepford Express (7) than Stepford Connect (5). Before V1.7.2, destination displays on the trains and Passenger Information Screens displayed the station as 'Llyn-by-the-Sea', with hyphens. As of V1.7.2, the hyphens have been removed, now displayed as 'Llyn by the Sea' instead. As of V2.0 , this is one of the five to have a lounge , being the second after Stepford Central . Others can be found at Stepford Airport Central , Westwyvern and Northshore . If a player is a Guard and go to main menu on duty and then selects a train stopped on one of showcased platforms, a message box appears with the text "Must be spawned to request guard". Many players have been asking for AirLink to stop at Llyn-by-the-Sea. Various staff members have stated this will not happen and that the station will only be served by Stepford Connect and Stepford Express , as this would just make Stepford Express obsolete. In response to this, on 1st April 2025, however, AirLink had their services extended to Llyn-by-the-Sea for April Fools' Day only. Routes that terminate at this station sometimes have poor timetables, especially when coming from Northshore Depot , causing on-time Drivers to have to wait multiple minutes at the terminating platform before being able to turn around or despawn. Passengers can take a direct Stepford Express train from here to 15 of its 16 stations (all except Eden Quay ). It is tied with Benton , Leighton City & Leighton Stepford Road in this matter. ## Station 43: Millcastle

**Page ID:** 6875
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Millcastle

**Summary:**
Millcastle is a through station on the Stepford Main Line that opened in Version 1.4 .

**Full Content:**

Millcastle Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Station View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone MLC E Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-4 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Llyn District Zone - Platforms 4 (2 in use) Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Millcastle Racecourse 0.36 miles / 591 metres Westercoast 1.2 miles / 1.93 kilometres Westwyvern 2.16 miles / 3.48 kilometres Track Layout to Westwyvern to Millcastle Racecourse Millcastle is a through station on the Stepford Main Line that opened in Version 1.4 . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Leighton City , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . Stepford Express , which runs along the Stepford Connect line, passes this station. History [ ] 2019 17 December - Version 1.4 Millcastle added to the network as part of the Llyn-by-the-Sea extension, as a Stepford Connect through station with 2 side platforms used by Stepford Connect and an island platform for Stepford Express . Stepford Express passes and does not stop here however. New routes: R024 , R025 & R026 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R035 , R036 , R037 & R038 29 October - Version 1.7 New route: R040 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Added Stepford Connect services to Leighton West . Route changes: R037 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Llyn-by-the-Sea ) R038 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Westwyvern ) Now terminates at Leighton City. New route: R042 2024 22 April Sneak peek for Millcastle's overhaul was released. Lets hope the signals don't reflect off that windscreen too much... 12 August - Version 2.0 Station overhauled, concourse is no longer located above the platforms. Now located near Platform 1, connected to all platforms using a footbridge. Platform layout is unchanged and Stepford Express still does not serve the station. Added Stepford Connect services to the Rayleigh Bay branch . New routes: R050 & R102 Trivia [ ] This station has step-free access. Platforms 2 and 3 are unused for unknown reasons. They are the passing platforms for Stepford Express , making this station part of a 5-way tie between this station, Whitney Green , Greenslade , Hampton Hargate and Millcastle Racecourse for the most unused platforms of any station. In the sneak peek of the upgraded Millcastle, there are benches on Platform 2 and 3. Some players speculated that the platforms may be used for services in V2.0 . However, this was not materialised, as they remain unused after the update. This station, along with Westwyvern , were the only two stations on the Llyn extension that were not revealed in any way on the SCR Official Discord server before opening. This station is next to multiple playing fields, which might mean that Millcastle is known for sports. It is possible to walk from this station to Millcastle Racecourse without trespassing . Despite the fact that Platforms 2 and 3 are unused, warning announcements still sound for Stepford Express trains passing those platforms. The same applies to Platforms 2 and 3 at Millcastle Racecourse . The distance between this station and Westwyvern is the longest distance between any two stations without any stations in between, measuring at 2.16 miles. The distance between Hampton Hargate and Water Newton was once the longest until Upper Staploe was added in between the two stations in V1.7 . Oddly, in the previous version of the station, one of the lights between the platforms under the concourse had 3 missing parts. Looking closely, where the old station used to be located can be seen, as the fountain and shops in that area remained the same. The light on the left is normal, while the one on the right has most of its parts missing Gallery [ ] Version 1.4 - V1.10.13 [ ] Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Unused Platforms View Stations Willowfield ‚Ä¢ Hemdon Park ‚Ä¢ Beechley ‚Ä¢ Stepford Victoria ‚Ä¢ Financial Quarter ‚Ä¢ City Hospital ‚Ä¢ Stepford Central ‚Ä¢ Stepford East ‚Ä¢ Stepford High Street ‚Ä¢ Whitefield Lido ‚Ä¢ Stepford United Football Club ‚Ä¢ Woodhead Lane ‚Ä¢ Houghton Rake ‚Ä¢ Whitefield ‚Ä¢ St Helens Bridge ‚Ä¢ New Harrow ‚Ä¢ Elsemere Pond ‚Ä¢ Elsemere Junction ‚Ä¢ Berrily ‚Ä¢ East Berrily ‚Ä¢ Beaulieu Park ‚Ä¢ Morganstown ‚Ä¢ Angel Pass ‚Ä¢ Bodin ‚Ä¢ Coxly ‚Ä¢ Benton ‚Ä¢ Port Benton ‚Ä¢ Benton Bridge ‚Ä¢ Stepford Airport Parkway ‚Ä¢ Stepford Airport Central ‚Ä¢ Airport Terminal 2 ‚Ä¢ Hampton Hargate ‚Ä¢ Upper Staploe ‚Ä¢ Water Newton ‚Ä¢ Winstree ‚Ä¢ Rocket Parade ‚Ä¢ Leighton Stepford Road ‚Ä¢ Leighton City ‚Ä¢ Leighton West ‚Ä¢ Rayleigh Bay ‚Ä¢ Carnalea Bridge ‚Ä¢ Aslockby ‚Ä¢ Edgemead ‚Ä¢ Faymere ‚Ä¢ Westercoast ‚Ä¢ Millcastle Racecourse ‚Ä¢ Millcastle ‚Ä¢ Westwyvern ‚Ä¢ Starryloch ‚Ä¢ Northshore ‚Ä¢ Llyn-by-the-Sea List of Stations ‚Ä¢ List of Stations (Statistics) ‚Ä¢ List of Station Codes Upcoming stations are marked in italics , former stations are marked in strikethrough . ## Station 44: Millcastle Racecourse

**Page ID:** 6585
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Millcastle_Racecourse

**Summary:**
Millcastle Racecourse is a limited-service through station on the Stepford Main Line near Millcastle .

**Full Content:**

Millcastle Racecourse Entrance Path to Station Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform View 4 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone MRC E Station headcode Dispatching - No Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Llyn District Zone - Platforms 4 (2 in use) Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines No Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Westercoast 0.84 miles / 1.35 kilometres Millcastle 0.36 miles / 591 metres Track Layout to Millcastle to Westercoast Millcastle Racecourse is a limited-service through station on the Stepford Main Line near Millcastle . It is served by Stepford Connect services to St Helens Bridge , Leighton City , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . The station also consists of two unused platforms for Stepford Express trains to pass by. Contents 1 Station layout 2 Services 3 Station announcements 4 History 5 Trivia 6 Notes 7 Gallery Station layout [ ] Stopping Passing G Path Footbridge to platforms, path to racecourse & exit G Platforms ‚Üí Stepford Connect to Westwyvern & Llyn-by-the-Sea ( MLC ) Platform 1 Platform 2 ‚Üí Stepford Express platform, not in use (See Passing ) ‚Üê Stepford Express platform, not in use (See Passing ) Platform 3 Platform 4 ‚Üê Stepford Connect to St Helens Bridge , Leighton City , Rayleigh Bay & Edgemead ( WST ) Legend ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound G Path Footbridge to platforms, path to racecourse & exit G Platforms ‚Üí Stepford Connect to Westwyvern & Llyn-by-the-Sea ( MLC ) Platform 1 Platform 2 ‚Üí Stepford Express to Westwyvern & Llyn-by-the-Sea ( WYV / NSE / LYN ) ‚Üê Stepford Express to Stepford Central , Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton & Rayleigh Bay ( WST / EDG / LTC ) Platform 3 Platform 4 ‚Üê Stepford Connect to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , Leighton City & Leighton West ( WST ) Legend ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound Services [ ] Platform(s) Previous station Route Next station 1 Westercoast R025 R038 R102 to Westwyvern Millcastle R040 R050 to Llyn-by-the-Sea 4 Millcastle R025 to St Helens Bridge Westercoast R038 to Leighton City R040 to Edgemead R050 R102 to Rayleigh Bay Station announcements [ ] Type Audio Platform https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:MRCP.mp3 https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:MRCC.mp3 N/A N/A https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:MRCE.ogg [ note 1 ] Please note: iOS and iPadOS do not natively support playing .ogg audio files and will show an error. History [ ] 2019 26 November Sneak peek for Millcastle Racecourse was released, in a signalling board. Christmas lights üéÑ 17 December - Version 1.4 Millcastle Racecourse added to the network as part of the Llyn-by-the-Sea extension, as a limited-service Stepford Connect through station with 2 side platforms used by Stepford Connect and an island platform for Stepford Express . Stepford Express passes and does not stop here however. New route: R025 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 New route: R038 29 October - Version 1.7 Added Stepford Connect services to Llyn-by-the-Sea . New route: R040 2021 19 November Sneak peek for Millcastle Racecourse's overhaul was released. Another little station upgrade that we thought we would do ready for v1.8... Probably not as difficult to work out which one this is üòâ Coming soon in v1.8 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled, new platforms, footbridge and station entrance, with lifts installed. The station is now step-free. Platforms are now 2 island platforms shared by Stepford Connect and Stepford Express . Route change: R038 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Westwyvern ) Now terminates at Leighton City. 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added to Platform 2 & 3. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Added Stepford Connect services to the Rayleigh Bay branch . New routes: R050 & R102 Trivia [ ] This station was first shown in a signalling board sneak peek on 28 November 2019. This is the second station to be near a stadium, with the first one being Stepford United Football Club . As of the V1.4 update, Platforms 2 and 3 are unused for unknown reason. They are the Stepford Express passing platforms, making this station part of a 5-way tie between Whitney Green , Greenslade , Hampton Hargate , this station, and Millcastle for the most unused platforms of any station at two. Of the eleven Stepford Connect routes that run through this station, only five of them ( R025 , R038 , R040 , R050 and R102 ) call here, making this station a limited-service station. Since V2.0 , players can walk from this station to Millcastle via road. Although Platforms 2 and 3 remain unused, the non-stop platform warning announcements for Stepford Express trains passing through the station are still sounded. The same applies to Platforms 2 and 3 at Millcastle . Stepford Express might have been intended to stop here, as this station has on-board announcements for the operator here. However, no announcements have been found for Stepford Express at Millcastle . The IET stop markers being added to the station in V1.10.8 further supports this, potentially meaning that Stepford Express might stop here in the future. However, this is not confirmed . Although being a non-dispatchable station, there are OFF indicators at this station for guards . Starryloch also shares this trait. The farthest station a passenger can get from this station on one train before requiring to change to another is St Helens Bridge . This station is the only station on the Stepford Main Line and one of the five Stepford Connect stations which do not have a route calling at Stepford Central , the others are Leighton West , Aslockby , Carnalea Bridge , and Rayleigh Bay . Upper Staploe used to have this trait as well until V1.8 , when R003 ( Stepford Central <> Leighton City ) started calling there. This station's name is the longest out of any other two-word-long station on the entire network, being twenty letters long. This station was made by Developer Thehazad9. There is a parked Class 68 at the station's siding. There is a part from an old light model on the approach path to the station underneath an existing light. The station is adjacent to the horse racecourse of the same name. This station has the biggest sign located on the Llyn side end of the platforms. ## Station 45: Morganstown

**Page ID:** 4897
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Morganstown

**Summary:**
Morganstown is a major through station and terminus that opened as part of Version 1.1 along with the Stepford Connect extension. Located at the end of the Morganstown Branch , this station serves Stepford Connect services to Stepford Central ; Metro services to Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central and St Helens Bridge ; Waterline services to Newry Harbour and Benton ; AirLink services to Stepford Central , Airport Terminal 2 and Airport Terminal 3 ; and Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry , Benton , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea .

**Full Content:**

Morganstown Entrance Concourse Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone MGT D Station headcode Dispatching M Yes (1 slot) P1-6 Electrification Line Yes (Platform 1-4) No (Platform 5-6) Morganstown Branch Station Information Location Morganstown District Zone - Platforms 7 Tracks 7 Accessibility Step-free access via ramps Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing None Service Information Preceding station Following station Morganstown Docks 0.41 miles / 660 metres Beaulieu Park 0.54 miles / 869 metres Berrily 1.9 mi / 3.1 km Benton 1.02 miles / 1.64 kilometres Elsemere Junction 2.4 miles / 3.86 kilometres St Helens Bridge 4.24 miles / 6.82 kilometres Terminus Stepford Airport Central 1.98 miles / 3.19 kilometres Leighton Stepford Road 4.72 miles / 7.59 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot - Morganstown Siding Airport Parkway Depot Morganstown is a major through station and terminus that opened as part of Version 1.1 along with the Stepford Connect extension. Located at the end of the Morganstown Branch , this station serves Stepford Connect services to Stepford Central ; Metro services to Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central and St Helens Bridge ; Waterline services to Newry Harbour and Benton ; AirLink services to Stepford Central , Airport Terminal 2 and Airport Terminal 3 ; and Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry , Benton , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . This station was overhauled in Version 1.7 and is now managed by National Rail . Prior to the station's upgrade, Morganstown was managed by Network Rail . This station will be receiving another major overhaul in Version 2.3 . History [ ] 2018 9 December Sneak peek for Morganstown was released, as part of Day 9 of the Advent Calendar. It's Day 9 and today we present another new station: Morganstown. Close to Morganstown Docks (Waterline), this station serves multiple lines including Connect and is along the same extension branch as Berrily (yesterday's sneak peek). All coming to the game in V1.1 üéÄ 31 December - Version 1.1 Morganstown added to the network as part of the Morganstown branch , as a major through station and terminus with 6 platforms, serving Stepford Connect and AirLink . New routes: R007 & R053 2019 1 February - Version 1.1.9 Added AirLink services to Airport Terminal 1 & 2 . Route change: R053 ( Stepford Central <> Stepford Airport Central ‚Üí Airport Terminal 2 (via T1 ) (S) ) Now stops at Airport Terminal 1 & 2. 2020 22 February - Version 1.4.1 Morganstown is now dispatchable. 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch ; and Waterline shuttle services to Benton . Platform 5A & 5B are now in use along with the Waterline shuttle service. New routes: R015 & R034 Bug : AirLink trains can sometimes be misdirected onto the Morganstown Flyover , and despawned at Morganstown Docks . This was quickly fixed later. 5 September Sneak peek for Morganstown's overhaul was released. Another station upgrade, courtesy of @[PDV] Thehazad9 , but where could it be? ü§î 29 October - Version 1.7 Station overhauled, a glass roof was added over the station. Concourse added under the station, with shops. Added Stepford Express services to Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . New routes: R080 & R082 Platform priorities added. SAC ‚Üí MGT P6, then P4 Bug : The signal at Platform 5B (W118) displays and stays stuck on Danger, even with no traffic. This is only visual. This was fixed later in an unknown date. 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Platform allocation is now randomised at P1-2, 4 & 6. Bug : Trains cannot close doors at Platform 5A & B, unless there is a Guard . 18 December - Version 1.8.1 Bugfix : Trains now can close doors normally at Platform 5A & B. 2022 15 May - Version 1.9 Added Stepford Express services to Newry and Benton . New routes: R083 & R085 Bug : Stepford Connect trains can sometimes be misdirected onto the Morganstown Flyover . A Class 377 on the flyover 17 May Bugfix : Stepford Connect trains now proceed to Beaulieu Park as normal. Bug : Stepford Connect trains may derail when entering Platform 1 & 2, and be despawned. Example of the derail bug 25 May - Version 1.9.1 Bugfix : Stepford Connect trains now enter Platform 1 & 2 normally. 27 August - Version 1.10 Added AirLink services to Airport Terminal 3 . New route: R058 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added to Platform 3, 4 & 6. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 An OFF indicator has been added at Platform 3 and banner repeaters have been added at Platform 5A & B for better visibility. Added Waterline services to Newry Harbour . New route: R120 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Added Metro services. New routes: R130 , R131 & R137 5 August - Version 2.2.1 A poster named "Network Expansion" was added next to the station entrance. This won the first Community Spotlight hosted in May 2025. 'Network Expansion' by exexexe5 22 October Sneak peek for Morganstown's upgrade was released, based on Stalybridge station . It's all change at this station and beyond. üåÜ üöÑ Coming to SCR version 2.3 Trivia [ ] Morganstown is the first, and currently the only, station to serve all five operators as of Version 2.2 . Before Metro , Morganstown was also the only station to serve all the other four operators since Version 1.7 . Despite this, Morganstown is often unused, as many AirLink and Stepford Express services skip this station and not many Stepford Connect , Metro and Waterline services terminate here, compared to Benton . This is one of two stations to have letter subdivided platforms (the other being Esterfield ). During parts of late 2019, the platform announcements were glitched when the station name was said. They were fixed in the Five Million Update . This also occurred at New Harrow and Berrily . Despite being a large station, there were no CIS Boards before V1.4.1 . The same was said for Berrily , but these were added in an earlier update. This station is the first Waterline - AirLink interchange, the second being Airport Terminal 2 . Morganstown Siding is located east of Morganstown, which leads to Platform 6. This siding can only used by R015 , R120 and R137 . AirLink trains can not spawn there, however. Due to the short length of the siding, which cannot fit most AirLink trains . The nearby Stepford Airport Parkway TMD is used instead. This station, as well as Westercoast and Willowfield , have the longest single-word station names, with the overall longest station name being Stepford United Football Club . Before the Morganstown Shuttle was opened in V1.6 , there were no direct rail connections between this station and Morganstown Docks . At that time, if a passenger wanted to go to Morganstown Docks from here, they needed to take a Stepford Connect service to Beaulieu Park , then walk to Whitney Green and take a Waterline train to Morganstown Docks . On 5 September 2020, Former Managing Director Charlie_RBX posted a preview of the upgraded Morganstown "courtesy of Thehazad9", but at the time the station was unknown. It was confirmed in the SCR Discord Signalling Lounge by former Operations Manager RLSJ1997 that it was Morganstown later that month. Although players can see Hampton Hargate from here with a high enough render distance, there is no direct link, so passengers have to travel via Leighton Stepford Road or Benton . Despite Morganstown being a major interchange station, it does not have ticket gates or card readers. On the Stepford Connect map, the Morganstown Connect routes shows its availability to go from Morganstown to Beechley. As of Version 2.2 , no Stepford Connect route exists that goes from Morganstown to Beechley nor from Berrily either. R034 (now used for Metro ) used to originally be a Stepford Connect route, which follows the Morganstown Connect route lines. Same goes for R030 . The 13 October 2025 sneak peek shows a double Class 350 /1 headed to Westwyvern via Elsemere Junction . This has led to speculation about an upgrade to the station connecting the Stepford Connect tracks to the Stepford Main Line . The overhauled Morganstown station which will be released in Version 2.3 is being criticised by the community mainly because of the removal of the canopy. Hence, players may call it a ‚Äòdowngrade‚Äô instead of an overhaul. Previous speculations & plans [ ] An intended operator called 'High Speed' that was planned to pass through Morganstown. But it was integrated with Stepford Express when services commenced to Morganstown in Version 1.7 . There used to be a part of the station called Morganstown High Level , which was just 2 elevated platforms. They had no connection to Morganstown station, but had a link to Morganstown Docks . Eventually, it was replaced by Platforms 5A and 5B, with the original platforms being demolished. It is possible that the Morganstown Shuttle was planned to terminate at Morganstown High Level. Prior to V1.7 , the rails at Platforms 1 and 2 extended noticeably beyond the buffers. Many players had speculated that there would be an extension for Stepford Connect on the Morganstown Branch, though this never happened. The sneak peek of the new driving HUD for V2.0 showed a Stepford Express service allocated to Platform 5 at Morganstown, leading players to believe the update would include a revamp of the station. This was later confirmed to be a mistake by Community Director tjh44 . ## Station 46: Morganstown Docks

**Page ID:** 452
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Morganstown_Docks

**Summary:**
Morganstown Docks is a through station served by Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton , Morganstown and Greenslade ; and limited Metro services to Stepford Victoria and Morganstown .

**Full Content:**

New route: R137 Trivia [ ] This station seems to be based off of the Dudley Port station in Tipton, Sandwell, West Midlands. This station has step-free access. With a gap of only 0.17 miles (274 metres), Morganstown Docks and Port Benton are the two closest stations on the whole network . Intially, the distance was a bit longer at 0.24 miles (386 metres). This beats Elsemere Pond and Elsemere Junction by 0.09 miles, which have a distance of 0.26 miles between the two stations. Because of the short distance between this station and Port Benton , there isn't enough time to play the "next station is" announcement between these stations. After closing the Waterline train doors on either this station or Port Benton , the train will immediately play "We will be shortly arriving at..." annoucement before the "Welcome on-board" announcement. It is possible to get off a train at this station, run to Port Benton , and catch the same train due to the short distance. Morganstown Docks is actually the newest station on the Greenslade Branch . Before it was added, trains just went between Port Benton to Whitney Green before Morganstown Docks was added between those two stations, making it an infill station. In Version 1.6 , the Morganstown Shuttle opened, and this station finally got a direct connection to Morganstown . Before that, if a player wanted to go from here to Morganstown , they would have to take a Waterline train to Whitney Green , then walk to Beaulieu Park , and then take a Stepford Connect service to Morganstown . Strangely, this station opened before the main Morganstown station. This station received a scenery update, with an actual dock next to the station in V1.7 . However, the station itself was not upgraded. Despite its name, this station is actually closer to Benton than it is to Morganstown , especially if the width of the River Ben is being taken into account. The platforms at this station are too short for the double Class 165 , 4-car Class 319 , 4-car Class 379 and 4-car Class 756 where the doors on the rear coach will not open. The announcement also plays on the Class 143 Double , despite all of the doors fitting on the platform. This is the only station that is managed by Waterline that Metro stops at. Despite the station lacking electrification, EMUs are still able to pass or serve the station. When driving a 3-car Class 195 , the driver will be prompted to move forward when the driver stopped at the S Car Marker perfectly. History [ ] 2018 12 December Sneak peek for New Harrow was released, as part of Day 12 of the Advent Calendar. It's Day 12 and I accidentally took this picture during the night time but nevermind üòÇ you can see how our new lighting looks at night too, so I suppose it's a double sneak peek. New route: R008 2019 20 January - Version 1.1.5 New Harrow is no longer dispatchable. 2020 15 April - Version 1.4.6 ( Ten Million Update ) New route: R027 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R008 , R130 , R131 , R132 , R133 , R134 , R135 & R136 Trivia [ ] The announcements for this station, as well as Berrily and Morganstown , used to glitch and kill the station's announcements. This was fixed in V1.3.29. There was going to be an Old Harrow station which was going to serve Metro , however, it was demolished and the line going through that station was lifted. This station's platforms are slightly shorter than the length of a 5-car train. When a 5-car train approaches this station, the announcer will state that the doors of the rear coach will not open. This also happens at Hemdon Park , Woodhead Lane , Elsemere Pond and East Berrily . The scenery upgrade in V1.7 has made New Harrow to become somewhat iconic due to the flyover right before the station, and it is a great place for trainspotting. The station building itself was also slightly updated, with a ramp added at the entrance. Before that, this station was wheelchair accessible for interchange only as you must use the short staircase at the entrance to access the station. The announcements for Platform 1 are known to play too early before the train arrives. This is likely due to the placement of the sensor much further away from the station. The same occurs for Platform 1 at Upper Staploe . This is one of the only stations to have a foot crossing. Platform 2 is inaccessible to pedestrians and pedestrians cannot exit from platform 2 whilst there is a longer train at platform 2 or a train at platform 1 overshoots. Notes [ ] ‚Üë This announcement was used in-game before the introduction of Metro , however, is no longer used. ## Station 48: Newry

**Page ID:** 5114
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Newry

**Summary:**
Newry is a terminus and through station on the Newry Branch .

**Full Content:**

Newry Overview West Entrance East Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Waiting Area (P3) Footbridge Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone NRY F Station headcode Dispatching N Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line Yes Newry Branch Station Information Location Benton District Zone Newry Zone Platforms 3 Tracks 5 Accessibility Level access & step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available at east entrance Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus Newry Harbour 0.64 miles / 1.03 kilometres Eden Quay 0.95 miles / 1.53 kilometres Benton 2.45 miles / 3.94 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot - Newry Siding Newry is a terminus and through station on the Newry Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Connolly , Airport Terminal 2 , Farleigh , Esterfield , Greenslade and Morganstown ; and Stepford Express services to Newry Harbour , Leighton City and Llyn-by-the-Sea . Newry's platform allocation is unique, as Waterline trains can terminate in any platform [ note 1 ] and Stepford Express trains can only terminate in Platform 2-3. Newry Harbour -bound trains can only use Platform 3 though. There are also unused passing tracks between Platform 2 and 3, reserved for possible future Waterline and Stepford Express routes and the "Return to depot" feature. Trivia [ ] This station is based on Newbury station . This station has step-free access. Before V1.9 , Newry was one of the two stations to have platforms divided by letters, along with Morganstown . Before V1.9 , trains at Platform 2B could not depart until a Waterline service from Newry Harbour arrived on Platform 1, due to the fact that the stretch between Newry Harbour and Newry is single-tracked. However, such a situation rarely occurred as very few drivers chose to drive R012 , the only service calling at Newry Harbour at the time. This can still happen at the current version of Newry, where trains will have to wait at Platform 3 if Newry Harbour either has both its platforms occupied or there is a train in the single-track section. In one of BanTech 's livestreams, the developers said that there is a possibility for a Newry Depot. However, a siding was materialized instead of a depot. This was one of the only three stations that was still using old banner repeaters along with St Helens Bridge and Bodin . These banner repeaters were later replaced in V1.4.1 . There is a station in real life with the same name in Northern Ireland. This station is one of four multi-line through stations that are always stopped at by every route that approaches it, with the others being Stepford Central , Benton and and Stepford Airport Central . This station is one of three stations served by Stepford Express but not Stepford Connect , the other two being Newry Harbour and Eden Quay . Before The Big Update , a sign at the entrance of the station stated that services went to 'Rose Dale Head', which later became Connolly . Some have predicted that a station in the James Street Extension may take that name, similar to how Beechley took City Hospital 's old name and Willowfield took Financial Quarter 's old name. This was partially confirmed with the opening of Rosedale Village in V1.10 . In V1.8.0 , there was a bug where trains could not close doors at Platforms 2A and 2B, making Newry Harbour inaccessible unless the train skipped Newry. This could be temporarily circumvented if the train has a Guard . Platforms 1 and 3 still worked as intended and doors could be closed. The same bug also happened at Morganstown Platform 5A and 5B. The bug was fixed in V1.8.1. When the first sneak peek for Newry's overhaul in V1.9 was released, even though the station's name was not confirmed at the time, the community highly speculated this station to be Newry. Some have also suspected the sneak peek is James Street instead, but the commercial buildings shown in the background are located near Newry, which made this less likely to be true. Later, a second sneak peek was released on 12 May 2022, which revealed that Stepford Express will be stopping and going to Newry and Newry Harbour . Furthermore, this also confirmed that the previous sneak peek is Newry (due to OFF indicators showing it is between " Harbour " and " Eden Quay "). This also explains the passing tracks in the previous sneak peek. Though after V1.9 released, the passing tracks are unused, possibly reserved for use in future updates. Gallery [ ] The unused Signal W064 at Newry before V1.4.1 The unused Signal W064 at Newry after V1.4.1 Pre- V1.9 Entrance Pre-V1.9 Platform View V1.9 Platform View Pre-V1.9 Platform 2B Notes [ ] ‚Üë Added in Version 1.10 , Waterline trains will prioritise Platform 1 first if it is empty, to avoid blocking traffic to and from Newry Harbour . ## Station 49: Newry Harbour

**Page ID:** 114
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Newry_Harbour

**Summary:**
Newry Harbour is a limited-service diesel-only terminus at the end of the Newry Branch .

**Full Content:**

Newry Harbour Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Harbour Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone NRH F Station headcode Dispatching H Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line No Newry Branch Station Information Location Benton District Zone Newry Zone Platforms 2 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via ramps Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus Newry 0.64 miles / 1.03 kilometres Newry Harbour is a limited-service diesel-only terminus at the end of the Newry Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Connolly , Farleigh and Morganstown ; and Stepford Express services to Llyn-by-the-Sea . Contents 1 Station layout 1.1 Legend 1.2 Note 2 Services 3 Station announcements 4 History 5 Trivia 6 Notes 7 Gallery Station layout [ ] G Platforms Unused track, merges with Platform 1 track ‚îú ‚ä¢ Waterline terminating platform ‚Üí Waterline to Connolly , Farleigh & Morganstown ( NRY ) ‚ä¢ Stepford Express terminating platform ‚Üí Stepford Express to Llyn-by-the-Sea ( NRY ) Platform 1 ‚Üê Exit to harbour Waiting shelter & ticket machines Exit to street ‚Üí Platform 2 ‚îú ‚ä¢ Waterline terminating platform ‚Üí Waterline to Connolly , Farleigh & Morganstown ( NRY ) ‚ä¢ Stepford Express terminating platform ‚Üí Stepford Express to Llyn-by-the-Sea ( NRY ) ‚îú Unused track G Harbour Parked VisitBodin cruise ship Legend [ ] ‚Üí Westbound ‚ä¢ Terminal ‚îú Buffer Note [ ] Longer trains can only terminate at Platform 1. History [ ] 2017 21 December Newry Harbour was added to the network as part of the Newry branch , as a limited Waterline terminus with 1 platform only. There is only a single track leading up to this station. On the same day, this station was made to allow diesel trains only to reduce congestion, banning the Class 387 temporarily. New route: Newry Harbour <> Greenslade 2018 21 April - Version 1.0 Added Waterline services to the Connolly branch . New route: R012 Route removal: Newry Harbour <> Greenslade Removed from the game. 4 December Sneak peek for Newry Harbour's scenery upgrade was released. welcome to Day 4! We've upgraded all the scenery around Newry Harbour ‚õÑ 31 December - Version 1.1 Scenery around the station was upgraded, with new commercial buildings . 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Bug : Trains cannot access Newry Harbour as trains cannot close doors at Newry Platform 2A & B, unless there is a Guard . 18 December - Version 1.8.1 Bugfix : Trains can now access Newry Harbour normally again. 2022 12 May Sneak peek for a Stepford Express train arriving at Newry from Newry Harbour was released. And there you were thinking that our social media post on April 1st was a joke... Coming soon... 15 May - Version 1.9 Station overhauled, platforms increased from 1 to 2. Now based on Kyle of Lochalsh station . Scenery near the station was upgraded, including a cruise ship near the harbour, connected to the harbour the station is on. Added Stepford Express services to the Llyn-by-the-Sea branch via Benton . New route: R084 Bug : Trains entering Newry from Newry Harbour will be despawned by the message "Buffers don't like to be eaten". 17 May Bugfix : Trains can now enter Newry normally. 27 August - Version 1.10 HST stop markers added to Platform 1 & 2. Added Waterline services to Farleigh . New route: R018 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added to Platform 1 & 2. 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 EMUs can no longer enter Newry Harbour. New route: R120 Trivia [ ] This station is based off the real life Kyle of Lochalsh station in the Highlands, northern Scotland. Prior to The Big Update , this station served Waterline services to and from Greenslade as Connolly was not in the game back then. For now, passengers willing to go to Greenslade should change at Newry , Benton or Morganstown Docks . Before Version 1.9 : This was the smallest station in SCR . This was one of the three stations in the game that only had 1 platform. The second one is Airport Terminal 1 and the third one is Leighton West . It was the only station in all of SCR to have the platform made entirely out of bricks. The station barely had any traffic, as Waterline was also not often driven by players then. This station's overhaul was not sneak peeked, but because of the overhaul of Newry and the confirmed extension of Stepford Express in Version 1.9 , it was highly anticipated for an overhaul. Due to the single track leading to this station, trains inbound to this station are forced to wait at Newry to allow outbound trains to free up the line. Waiting times of around three minutes may occur, however are unlikely since the station, if not the entirety of the Waterline network, remains seldom visited by drivers . This is the only limited service station that is a terminus. In V1.1 , scenery for this station was updated, adding many commercial buildings including a customs and shipping centre. These buildings still exist but were moved along with new scenery in Version 2.0 . It was originally intended that services to James Street would run from here, but the developers wanted to keep the station "tiny" in every way possible: the number of platforms and the number of services that arrive there. Ironically in V1.9 , a second platform was added, and Stepford Express services started to call here. And in V1.10 , a route was added to terminate at the new Farleigh station, one stop past James Street , where trains were originally meant to terminate at prior to the extension. There is a commercial building nearby named "Haughton Foundry", the name of the group that made Mind the Gap . This is one of the only stations with one track leading to it (alongside the Rayleigh Bay Branch , Airport Terminal 1 and Leighton West ). This station, alongside Morganstown Docks , were the only two stations that had dashed lines on the system map before V1.6 . This station was served mostly by 4-car Waterline trains since The Big Update , which were the Class 165/1 , Class 319 and Class 379 . The Class 387 served this station until it got moved to AirLink , and the Class 701 also served this station until it got removed in V1.1 . After the release of V2.0 , EMUs, namely Class 319 and Class 379 , are restricted from driving into this station, as electrification equipment is not implemented at this section. Also, the introduction of R120 , encourages 2-car trains serving this station. Near this station, there are tracks under a portal crane near a port, that include killblocks and buffers . This, the so-called "Platform 0" at Stepford Central (before a functioning Platform 0 was added at the station) and the addition of the static Class 66 Locomotives being added to Stepford Airport Parkway in V1.10 have made many players expecting a Freight line in SCR, though the developers have revealed nothing about this or if it will happen. Though this may all just be for scenery purposes only, as Stepford Airport Parkway is heavily based on the real life station Bristol Parkway , which has a freight siding next to it. In V1.6 , the route maps (both the Waterline one and the whole network one) labelled this stop as a station with limited service, probably due to a very small number of trains calling here. This station is one of two stations on the Waterline map to be considered limited service, the other being Rosedale Village . Prior to V1.10 , this station was the only limited service Waterline station. In contrary, after the Morganstown Shuttle of Waterline was introduced in V1.6 , though there are also not many trains serving the Morganstown Shuttle service, the Waterline map did not label Morganstown as a station with a limited service. [ note 1 ] However, in V1.10 , James Street also became a limited-service station [ note 2 ] , and a new limited-service station opened, Rosedale Village . In V1.9 , a cruise ship was added to the harbour along with the station's overhaul. However, it is solely for scenery purposes. This is the only place where players can see a cruise ship. Others are either container ships or private yachts. The river that empties to the left of Newry Harbour is the same river that cuts through downtown Stepford and Houghton Rake (though now not-fully covered by ground and tunnel), therefore the player can actually walk from Newry Harbour to Houghton Rake all the way to Stepford Central and Stepford Victoria by only following this river. Before reaching Houghton Rake , there is a branch that becomes its own river, the same river that cuts through St Helens Bridge . This station does not have electrification and thus can be only accessed by diesel-powered trains. However, before Version 2.0 , electric trains were allowed to drive into this station. Before The Big Update the station had diesel-only service, the Class 387 (operated by Waterline at the time) could not enter Newry Harbour, only allowing Class 165 and Class 166 trains. Notes [ ] ‚Üë A limited-service station often means that trains could have stopped at the limited-service station, but does not. Example being Rosedale Village , where R014 ( Newry <> Esterfield ) could have stopped there, but skips it instead. Being a limited-service station also requires at least two routes passing/stopping at that station, with at least 50% of the routes not stopping at it. Therefore, Morganstown is not considered as a limited-service station as all services that run there ( R015 and R120 ) stop here. In addition, Morganstown is also a major station. ‚Üë Even though James Street is shown as a limited service-station on the main network map but not on the Waterline operator map, it is to show clearly that there are services that skips James Street on the main network map. Though because 2 of the 3 routes stop at this station (and not less than 50% of routes, as mentioned above), this station is not shown as limited in the Waterline operator map. ## Station 50: Northshore

**Page ID:** 5763
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Northshore

**Summary:**
Northshore is an elevated through station on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

Northshore Main Entrance Main Entrance Interior Northshore Beach Entrance Subway Platform View 1 Platform View 2 The Lounge Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone NSE E Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-4 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Llyn District Zone - Platforms 4 Tracks 5 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Starryloch 0.8 miles / 1.29 kilometres Westwyvern 2.19 miles / 3.52 kilometres Westercoast 4.80 miles / 7.72 kilometers Leighton City 8.39 miles / 13.5 kilometres Llyn-by-the-Sea 1.76 miles / 2.83 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot Faymere Green SB Depot - Northshore is an elevated through station on the Stepford Main Line . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , Leighton City , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry , Benton , Rayleigh Bay and Llyn-by-the-Sea . Based on Stockport station . Northshore is now shown in the intro , replacing Airport West . Station upgraded, now includes The Lounge as well as scenery improvements. Northshore is no longer shown in the intro , replaced by Faymere Green TMD . Added Stepford Connect & Stepford Express services to Rayleigh Bay . New routes: R050 & R087 Trivia [ ] This station resembles Stockport railway station , although its location is similar to Dawlish railway station and Colwyn Bay railway station . This station is step-free as of V1.9 . Before that, it was the only Stepford Express station that did not have step-free access to any of its platforms. It was also previously one of the three Stepford Connect stations that did not have wheelchair access to platforms. The other two are Water Newton and Stepford Airport Parkway . But in V1.10 and V2.0 respectively, both stations have been made step-free as well. This is the first, and so far the only station to be directly connected to a beach or an ocean. Starryloch does not count, as the player is required to take the footbridge in order to get next to the beach. This station, along with Starryloch and Llyn-by-the-Sea , is roughly parallel to the Stepford Central - Morganstown - Leighton Stepford Road line. Before V1.7.2, this station was one of two stations that had a Platform 0, the other being Stepford Airport Central . After that, the platforms were changed from 0, 1, 2, 3 to 1, 2, 3, 4 and a Platform 0 was added to Llyn-by-the-Sea . This station has been praised by numerous players, as they say it has a very modern design. Northshore is the only elevated station on the Llyn line. This was the third station to have the National Rail Double Arrow symbol with its station name displayed at the entrances. This can also be found at Stepford Airport Central , Rosedale Village and Westercoast . Formerly, Leighton Stepford Road also shared this trait, but it was removed with the station remodelling in V1.8 . Northshore is one of the best places for sunset viewing, due to its empty beach and the ocean exit facing southwest. With V1.7.2, Northshore gained a passing track for Stepford Express services towards Stepford Central , being one of the three stations that has a passing track going in one direction. The other two are Elsemere Junction and Angel Pass . This station's distance from Starryloch is bizarre, as unlike other stations on the Llyn branch, it is less than a mile away, therefore it is prone to being overshot and on rare occasions skipped entirely by accident since most stations on the Llyn branch require trains to go at high speeds and long distances to get to the next station. Before V2.0 , this station still had Metro -red theming with all other stations having generic white or black or coloured to their main operator. This was eventually replaced with Stepford Express theming. This was the last place in SCR to retain the first version of the ticket machine decals , which were still seen at the beach entrance to the station. Eventually, they were replaced by the new meshed (second and current version) ticket machine decals. The first version of these decals were last seen in Northshore . The Information signs in the main concourse still have the old Stepford Express colour scheme. This was removed with the upgrade in V2.0 . The lamps at the beach entrance to this station are one of the last lamp models from before V1.4.1 . The same models can also be found at most Tramlink stops and at the ramp leading to Westercoast station. The old lamp prop in Northshore. Northshore is the third station to be operated by Stepford Express , after Leighton Stepford Road and Westwyvern . As well as the fourth station to have a lounge . Prior to Version 2.0 , it was one of the three Stepford Connect -managed stations that are served by Stepford Express , the others being Edgemead and Westercoast . The Stepford Connect station sign at the western entrance of Northshore station. Oddly, a Stepford Connect station sign could still be found near the station's car park in V2.0 , even though the station is now operated by Stepford Express . Additionally, dispatchers spawned at this station would still wear the Stepford Connect -branded uniforms. These were fixed in V2.0.1. The Northshore Depot is accessible from this station. ## Station 51: Old Harrow

**Page ID:** 17910
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Old_Harrow

**Summary:**
Cancelled feature

**Full Content:**

Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Old Harrow Operational Information Served by Managed by Metro (proposed) Metro Station code OHW Service Information Preceding station Following station St Helens Park St Helens South Old Harrow was a proposed station to be part of Metro . However, due to the cancellation of Metro, the station was demolished in The Big Update . Return speculation [ ] With Metro 's return in Version 2.2 , many players speculated that the original Metro Loop could return along with the previously proposed stations. However, the Metro Loop did not return and a new loop including Coxly Newtown was added instead. It is unknown if an introduction of the Metro Loop is planned in the future. Trivia [ ] This station was part of the former Metro Loop , which has been demolished as part of The Big Update . The only stations which remained in the game were Stepford Victoria , City Hospital (under the name Beechley) and Willowfield (nowadays Financial Quarter ). These stations would later become the Stepford Victoria Branch .

================================================================================

## Station 52: Port Benton

**Page ID:** 189
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Port_Benton

**Summary:**
Port Benton is a station on the Greenslade Branch .

**Full Content:**

Port Benton Entrance Concourse Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone PBN F Station headcode Dispatching P Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line No Wires not installed Greenslade Branch Station Information Location Benton District Zone Benton Zone Platforms 3 Tracks 3 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Benton 0.5 mi / 0.8 km Terminus Morganstown Docks 0.2 mi / 0.3 km Port Benton is a station on the Greenslade Branch . It is a terminus for limited Stepford Connect services from Willowfield ; and Metro services from Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central and St Helens Bridge . As well as a through station for Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Newry , Benton , Morganstown and Greenslade ; and limited Metro services to Stepford Victoria and Morganstown . New routes: R015 , R032 & R035 2021 17 October Sneak peek for Port Benton's overhaul was released. It's already #SneakPeekSunday again! A few other bits and bobs coming to v1.8, including a station overhaul and another train upgrade! 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled, new station building, platforms are now open instead of being indoors. Lift access added, Port Benton is now fully step-free. Platform 2 & 3 swapped roles, P2 now serves Waterline services to Benton and P3 serves Stepford Connect services instead. 2022 15 May - Version 1.9 Stepford Express services can now pass this station (does not stop). 27 August - Version 1.10 Bug : Stepford Connect trains cannot terminate at Platform 3. 2023 15 January - Version 1.10.3 Bugfix : Stepford Connect trains can now terminate again. 2 April - Version 1.10.7 New route: R047 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Added Waterline services to Newry Harbour . New route: R120 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Platform 3 can now serve as a bypass/overflow to Platform 2. Added Metro services. New route: R137 Trivia [ ] Port Benton and Morganstown Docks are only 0.17 miles (0.27 kilometres) apart, the shortest distance between two stations in the whole SCR network. As a result, the "Welcome onboard..." announcement plays immediately after "We will shortly be arriving...". Before Waterline services started calling here, Port Benton only had one Platform that was isolated from the rest of the line. This made it the smallest station in the game until the Waterline services opened. Port Benton, Airport Terminal 2 and Morganstown are the only stations where Dispatchers can dispatch both Stepford Connect and Waterline services. Players can walk from Port Benton to Morganstown Docks via road. Prior to V1.7 , players could also walk to Benton , Benton Bridge and Cambridge Street Parkway by road before the Benton District's redevelopment cut off access. This is the only Stepford Connect managed station that is served by Metro and Waterline . Before V1.5 , where Waterline was a subfranchise of Stepford Connect , Port Benton uniquely had white signs instead of the usual dark blue, suggesting it was "more Stepford Connect (Connect) than Waterline ". Additionally, Dispatcher spawned with the Connect uniform. Oddly, only one Stepford Connect route serve this station. Yet, Stepford Connect still manages this station as of V2.2 . Before V1.8 , the loop line from Port Benton to Benton was overgrown. It also used to have an old speed limit signs that seem to date back to the days of British Rail. This was removed in V1.9 . Before V1.7 , Port Benton was not near any port. After that, a major container port was added nearby to the station. Until its overhaul in V1.8 , this station did not have a concourse, and the main entrance was only a doorway to Platform 1. This station shares the headcode "P" with Stepford Airport Parkway . The other headcode sharing pairs of stations are Leighton Stepford Road and Rayleigh Bay (R), and Benton and Barton (B). Signals W016 and W018 on Platforms 2 and 3 going towards the Benton crossover have left feather indicators, which only light up when the train on these platforms is a Class 756 doing R137 . This is the only station in the Greenslade Branch that has Connect services. There is a bug that despawns a train that is leaving Platform 3 when heading to Benton from Morganstown Docks. ## Station 53: Rayleigh Bay

**Page ID:** 23053
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Rayleigh_Bay

**Summary:**
Rayleigh Bay is the terminus of the Rayleigh Bay Branch .

**Full Content:**

Rayleigh Bay Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone RLB H Station headcode Dispatching R Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line No Rayleigh Bay Branch Station Information Location Leighton District Zone - Platforms 3 Tracks 3 Accessibility Step-free access via ramps Ticket machines No, but ticket office available Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus Carnalea Bridge 0.52 miles / 0.84 kilometres Edgemead 0.89 miles / 1.43 kilometres Track Layout to Carnalea Bridge Rayleigh Bay is the terminus of the Rayleigh Bay Branch . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Leighton City , Leighton West , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Stepford Express services to Llyn-by-the-Sea . It was added along with Aslockby and Carnalea Bridge in Version 2.0 . The Rayleigh Bay Signal Box , which controls Zone H, is located east of this station. Something old, something new, something red, something blue. 12 August - Version 2.0 Rayleigh Bay added to the network as part of the Rayleigh Bay branch , as a Stepford Connect terminus with 3 platforms. New routes: R049 , R050 , R100 , R101 , R102 & R087 Trivia [ ] This station resembles Bradford Forster Square . This is one of three stations managed by Stepford Connect to be served by Stepford Express , with the others being Edgemead and Westercoast . This station shares the headcode "R" with Leighton Stepford Road . The other headcode sharing pairs of stations are Port Benton and Stepford Airport Parkway (P), and Benton and Barton (B). This station is the least used Stepford Express station, according to the Hub Site . This station has a small siding with a parked Class 68 with two locomotives ( Class 43 on the other end) and a single passenger car as decoration. Interestingly, the locomotive facing the station has Stepford Connect livery, and the other two cars facing away from the station have Stepford Express livery. This is especially notable due to the fact that Stepford Express does not operate Class 68s. The station's OFF indicators are tinted slightly yellow compared to the rest of the network's OFF indicators. The yellow OFF indicators at the station This station is one of the five Stepford Connect stations which do not have a route calling at Stepford Central , the others are Leighton West , Millcastle Racecourse , Carnalea Bridge , and Aslockby . ## Station 54: Robinson Way

**Page ID:** 7509
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Robinson_Way

**Summary:**
Unused feature

**Full Content:**

Unused feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed and added to the game, but ultimately left unused. Unused feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed and added to the game, but ultimately left unused. Robinson Way Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone ROW N/A Station headcode Dispatching N/A N/A Electrification Line Yes Greenslade Branch Station Information Location Morganstown District Platforms 2 Tracks 4 Accessibility Not step-free Service Information Preceding station Following station Whitney Green 0.43 miles / 692 metres (Not in service) Greenslade 0.47 miles / 756 metres (Not in service) Robinson Way is an abandoned and unused station located between Whitney Green and Greenslade . Waterline trains pass by the station on the tracks next to it, which has no platforms on it and does not stop at this station. The station and the tracks are on a private right of way. Since Version 1.7 , this is one of only three remaining Tramlink stations in-game, and the only one to not be served by Waterline . It is also one of two disused stations remaining from legacy plans, along with Upper Staploe (Metro) . Players can access the station by following the road from either Whitney Green or Greenslade . It is quicker to walk from Whitney Green, taking 2 minutes and 31 seconds, whereas it is 3 minutes and 14 seconds from Greenslade. ## Station 55: Rocket Parade

**Page ID:** 4937
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Rocket_Parade

**Full Content:**

Rocket Parade Entrance Concourse Track View Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone RCP D Station headcode Dispatching - No Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Leighton District Zone Leighton Zone Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Water Newton 1.0 mi / 1.6 km Leighton Stepford Road 0.5 mi / 0.8 km Rocket Parade is a through station located on the Stepford Main Line . New routes: R009 , R024 & R044 2022 27 February - Version 1.8.2 New route: R045 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Rocket Parade is no longer shown in the intro , replaced by Faymere Green TMD & Llyn-by-the-Sea . Trivia [ ] This station is based on Five Ways station , in Birmingham, England. This station has step-free access. Across from this station is BanTech Systems HQ. BanTech Systems used to work in association with Charlie_RBX , the former Managing Director , to develop Stepford County Railway as an Innovations Director . Prior to V1.1 , this station was the only limited-service station on the network . This station is discretely named after BanTech, the " Rocket " in Rocket Parade is a reference to the fact that BanTech studied rocket science at university. "Parade" is a common suffix. This station was the only one to remain in every iteration of the intro to the game. As the BanTech Systems Headquarters is outside this station, and SCR is a collaboration with BanTech Systems. However following BanTech 's resignation as Innovations Director , Rocket Parade has since been removed from V2.0 onwards. Before V1.8 , players could walk from here to Leighton Stepford Road . Players can still walk from here to Leighton Depot but the road cuts off right before reaching Leighton Stepford Road . The only way to get towards Leighton Stepford Road is by jumping over a fence. Strangely, there are no platform number signs at this station. This station has a lift to both platforms, but only Platform 2 has a direct lift from the concourse, while Platform 1 has a separate lift. Both lifts are connected with a footbridge on the mezzanine floor. Before the Leighton Zone replaced Winstree , it was located right where BanTech Systems HQ currently is, near this station. In a Directors Q&A on 23 October 2021, Managing Director Charlie_RBX has stated that more services will be scheduled to stop here in V1.8 . Eventually, R009 and R024 started calling here in V1.8, and this station is no longer considered as limited-service station. Even though it is no longer a limited-service station, there are still a few Stepford Connect routes that skip it, such as R004 and R035 . There is a big commercial building near Rocket Parade called RLSJ's Tuition Centre , however the building was not present in the sneak peek of the station's overhaul. ## Station 56: Rosedale Village

**Page ID:** 19958
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Rosedale_Village

**Summary:**
Rosedale Village is a limited-service through station on the Esterfield Branch .

**Full Content:**

Rosedale Village Northside Entrance Southside Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone RDV G Station headcode Dispatching - No Electrification Line Yes Esterfield Branch Station Information Location Farleigh District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Level access & step-free access via ramp Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Farleigh 1.0 mi / 1.6 km Esterfield 1.1 mi / 1.8 km Preceding depot Following depot - Esterfield Mainline Depot Rosedale Village is a limited-service through station on the Esterfield Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Benton and Esterfield . This station was released along with Farleigh and Esterfield as part of the Waterline Extension in Version 1.10 . Rosedale Village is only served by 1 route, being R016 ( Benton <> Esterfield ). The other route to Esterfield , R014 ( Newry <> Esterfield ) , skips this station. Contents 1 Station layout 2 Services 3 Station announcements 4 History 5 Trivia 6 Gallery Station layout [ ] Stopping Passing G Platforms Northside exit & ticket machine; footbridge to Platform 2 Platform 1 ‚Üí Waterline to Esterfield ( EFD ) ‚Üê Waterline to Benton ( FAR ) Platform 2 Southside exit & ticket machines; footbridge to Platform 1 Legend ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound G Platforms Northside exit & ticket machine; footbridge to Platform 2 Platform 1 ‚Üí Waterline to Esterfield ( EFD ) ‚Üê Waterline to Newry ( FAR ) Platform 2 Southside exit & ticket machines; footbridge to Platform 1 Legend ‚Üê Eastbound ‚Üí Westbound Services [ ] Platform(s) Previous station Route Next station 1 Farleigh R016 to Esterfield Esterfield 2 Esterfield R016 to Benton Farleigh Station announcements [ ] Type Audio Platform https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:RDVPL.mp3 N/A N/A https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:RDVWL.mp3 N/A Please note: iOS and iPadOS do not natively support playing .ogg audio files and will show an error. To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2022 27 August - Version 1.10 Rosedale Village added to the network as part of the Waterline extension , as a limited-service Waterline through station, with services to Benton and Esterfield only. Resembles Stansted Mountfitchet station . New route: R016 Trivia [ ] This station resembles Stansted Mountfitchet station in Essex. This station was never sneak peeked prior to its release. Prior to Version 2.0 , this was one of two stations to be considered limited service on the Waterline map, the other being Newry Harbour . In V1.10 , this station, along with James Street , were the first two stations to be skipped by Waterline services, as R014 ( Newry <> Esterfield ) skips both stops. The name 'Rosedale' comes from Connolly 's planned name, 'Rose Dale Head'. This is a similar situation to Willowfield and Beechley which were both the planned names for Financial Quarter and City Hospital respectively. This is the only Waterline station to not get Waterline services to Newry . Rosedale Village is barely used, as only R016 ( Benton <> Esterfield ) stops here. This makes it the only station to only have one route serving it (as of V2.2 ). Some players thought that the announcements for this station and Farleigh sounded unnatural as they did not fit well with other stations' announcements. Though Esterfield was not one of them as the announcements for the station was found as early as 2021, which was probably recorded together with the other stations. This station is the least used Waterline station and the second least used station in the entire game, according to the Hub Site . This station has the National Rail Double Arrow symbol on the southside entrance sign. It can also be found at Stepford Airport Central , Northshore and Westercoast . It is possible to walk to Water Newton from here via road without trespassing within a few minutes. ## Station 57: St Helens Bridge

**Page ID:** 434
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/St_Helens_Bridge

**Summary:**
St Helens Bridge (pronounced as Saint Helens Bridge ) is an elevated major through station located on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

St Helens Bridge Entrance Interior 1 Interior 2 Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform View 4 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SHB B Station headcode Dispatching I Yes (2 slots) P1-5 , P6-7 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Stepford District Zone Stepford City Zone Platforms 7 Tracks 7 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus Stepford East 1.17 miles / 1.88 kilometres Stepford High Street 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Stepford Central 2.26 miles / 3.64 kilometres Angel Pass 0.64 miles / 1.03 kilometres New Harrow 0.76 miles / 1.22 kilometres Bodin 1.07 miles / 1.72 kilometres Elsemere Junction 1.59 miles / 2.56 kilometres Berrily 2.24 miles / 3.6 kilometres Benton 3.3 miles / 5.31 kilometres Morganstown 4.26 miles / 6.85 kilometres Stepford Airport Parkway 4.7 miles / 7.56 kilometres (From Airport Parkway only) Preceding depot Following depot - Airport Parkway Depot St Helens Bridge (pronounced as Saint Helens Bridge ) is an elevated major through station located on the Stepford Main Line . It is a major interchange for Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , Morganstown , Port Benton , Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 , Leighton City , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , Berrily , Morganstown , Barton and Port Benton ; AirLink services to Stepford Central , Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 and Airport Terminal 3 ; and Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Benton , Leighton City and Llyn-by-the-Sea . St Helens Bridge underwent major overhauls in Version 1.0 and Version 1.10.7, as well as a platforms and scenery upgrade in Version 1.3.18. New routes: R047 & R048 2024 24 December - Version 2.1 New route: R088 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Platform 4 is now bi-directional, as an overflow to Platform 3 & 5. Added Metro services. New routes: R130 , R131 , R132 , R133 , R134 , R135 , R136 & R137 Trivia [ ] This station resembles Stratford station , located in London. This station is one of the 4 stations on the network managed by Transport for Stepford . Along with Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central and Stepford East . Before the Whitefield branch was introduced in V1.2 , every Stepford Connect route stopped here. This is one of the few stations that use both banner repeaters and OFF indicators. This is one of the most popular dispatching locations in the game along with Stepford East . One dispatcher can dispatch the vast majority of Stepford Connect and Metro services, as well as some Stepford Express trains. Currently, this station is one of the 4 quadrouple-line junctions alongside Stepford Central , Elsemere Junction and Benton . The 77 arch-viaduct used by Stepford Express for services via Benton to the north-east of the station was built by FirstManchester135 and MAGICMOVIESTEAM1 . It took them 4 hours and 32 minutes to build (excluding breaks), according to a plaque that was placed on 24 November 2017 at 8:41 PM. The plaque has since been removed. This viaduct used to lack in scenery until V1.7 when a small village was added under the viaduct. The speed limit for Stepford Express trains used to be 75 MPH, but it was increased to 90 MPH. In V1.7 , a new arch-viaduct was made for Stepford Express trains that go via the Morganstown Branch . This station was on Mattyx2013 's sneak peek showing new game lighting. The new lighting at St Helens Bridge Platform 1 used to be hard to access from other platforms before the tunnel was added. Being quite far away, this required dispatchers to walk a while just to get between Platform 1 and Platform 2-4, causing potential delays. Out of any station, this station has the most stations that players can get to directly from it, at 10. Lots of extra spare rails and cables can be seen at the end of the tracks acting as scenery. Equipment laid on the ballast spelling out "T J H 4 4" At the end of Platform 4 & 5, some of the equipment spell out "T J H" with 4 cable reels and 4 lined up rails. This is a reference to the Community Director tjh44, who did the overhaul of the station. This station is one of the first stations to include Roblox immersive advertisements, released just a few days prior to the V1.10.7 update.
