## Station 58: St Helens Park

**Page ID:** 17795
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/St_Helens_Park

**Summary:**
Cancelled feature

**Full Content:**

Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. St Helens Park Operational Information Served by Managed by Metro (presumably) Metro (presumably) Station code SHP Service Information Preceding station Following station Angel Pass St Helens Bridge St. Helens Park was a proposed station for Metro on the Stepford Main Line , and was situated just outside of St. Helens Bridge station. The station was demolished along with the rest of the Metro Loop in V1.0 . Return speculation [ ] With Metro 's return in Version 2.2 , many players speculated that the original Metro Loop could return along with the previously proposed stations. However, the Metro Loop did not return and a new loop including Coxly Newtown was added instead. It is unknown if an introduction of the Metro Loop is planned in the future. Trivia [ ] If this station did open, it would be one of the only stations with "Park" in its name, along with Hemdon Park , Beaulieu Park and Ashlan Park . The outlines where the platforms would've been can be clearly seen, East of St. Helens Bridge.

================================================================================

## Station 59: St Helens South

**Page ID:** 17911
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/St_Helens_South

**Summary:**
Cancelled feature

**Full Content:**

Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. St. Helens South Operational Information Served by Managed by Metro (proposed) Metro Station code STS Service Information Preceding station Following station Old Harrow Stepford Southgate St. Helens South was a proposed station to be part of Metro . However, due to the cancellation of Metro, the station was demolished in The Big Update . Return speculation [ ] With Metro 's return in Version 2.2 , many players speculated that the original Metro Loop could return along with the previously proposed stations. However, the Metro Loop did not return and a new loop including Coxly Newtown was added instead. It is unknown if an introduction of the Metro Loop is planned in the future. Trivia [ ] This station was part of the former Metro Loop , which was demolished within The Big Update except for Stepford Victoria and Willowfield (now called Financial Quarter ), which became the Stepford Victoria Branch. The station signs originally said "St. Helen ' s South", with an apostrophe.

## Station 60: Starryloch

**Page ID:** 5981
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Starryloch

**Summary:**
Starryloch is a limited-service through station on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

It is served by Stepford Connect services to Stepford Central , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead and Llyn-by-the-Sea . It was revealed on 16 October 2019, and opened on 17 December 2019 in Version 1.4 . This station will be receiving a minor upgrade in Version 2.3 . This is by far my favourite contribution to the game and I hope you love it as much as I do! üòç 17 December - Version 1.4 Starryloch added to the network as part of the Llyn-by-the-Sea extension, as a Stepford Connect through station with 2 side platforms with 2 express tracks between. Coming to SCR version 2.3 Trivia [ ] This station resembles Dawlish Warren station in Devon. The Class 68 / 444 exclusive routes, R026 and R036 , skip this station. However, they will still pass through the platforms while skipping this station, instead of using the Stepford Express passing tracks like Faymere . This is due to the two services having to call at Westwyvern and Northshore , and there are no points for them to switch to and from the express tracks between the two aforementioned stations. R037 (Leighton City <> Llyn-by-the-Sea) also skips this station. It is the only non-exclusive route to not stop here. Although this station is a limited service station, ironically 4 out of 7 Stepford Connect routes stop here. This is unrealistic especially considering that only 1 of the 3 routes that skip this station are non-exclusive. In the sneak peek for this station, you can distinctly see a purple train, which was later revealed to be a Class 43 . The shore starts coming into view near this station. On the platforms it is hard to see the shore as there is a forest between the station and beach. This station has an old-fashioned signal box, this is the Starryloch Signal Box . Before V1.7 , the signal box was purely for scenery and was non-functional. Between V1.7 and V1.7.2, the Zone E Signalling Desk was placed here before it was relocated to Llyn-by-the-Sea Rail Operations Centre Strangely, the empty signal box can still be accessed by Signallers in role. This is one of former Operations Director / Product Developer Mattyx2013's favourite stations, along with West Benton . On the Stepford Connect billboard, there is an advertisement for the commercial building , West Benton Pet Supplies. Other stations that used to have this ad were Leighton City and Whitefield Lido . Whitefield still has this advertisement. Although this station is not dispatchable, there are still OFF indicators here. This is also true for several stations, such as Rocket Parade and Millcastle Racecourse . It is speculated that the indicators were added to make guarding easier. Version 1.7.2 saw the footbridge extended to a sea wall, which you can walk along, as part of the scenery upgrade for Westwyvern . Because of this, it has become possible to walk between Starryloch and Westwyvern without having to step onto the baseplate. Platform 1 is featured in the SCR Prototyping Centre‚Äé‚Äé and the SCR Concept stall at Transport Tech 2021 , which showcases a new guarding procedure with keybinds, plus a physical guard panel in the train, along with keybinds to sit and open doors. There is a caravan park which is a short walk from the station. On one of the holiday homes, there was an image of Zippy, a puppet featured on Rainbow , posted on a window. However, this has since been removed in V1.9 for unknown reasons (possibly because of copyright). ## Station 61: Stepford Airport Central

**Page ID:** 8678
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Stepford_Airport_Central

**Summary:**
Stepford Airport Central (commonly known as Airport Central ) is a major terminus located in the Airport Zone , with through services to the airport terminals. It is served by Stepford Connect services to Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge and Airport Terminal 2 ; AirLink services to Stepford Central , Airport Terminal 2 , Airport Terminal 3 and Leighton Stepford Road ; and AirLink Shuttle services to Stepford Airport Parkway and Airport Terminal 2 .

History [ ] 2017 25 November Stepford Airport Central added to the network, as a major terminus with 7 platforms. Platform 0-2 is for Stepford Connect and Platform 3-6 is for AirLink . Platform 3-6 remained unused until AirLink was opened later in Version 1.1 . Added Stepford Connect services to Stepford Victoria ; and AirLink services to Stepford Central . New route: R052 Route change: R053 ( Stepford Central <> Stepford Airport Central ‚Üí Airport Terminal 2 (via T1 ) (S) ) Now stops at Airport Terminal 1 & 2. 2 February - Version 1.1.10 Added AirLink services to Airport Terminal 3 . New route: R055 16 September - Version 1.3.26 (Five Million Update) Added AirLink services to Leighton Stepford Road . New routes: R056 & R057 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to Beechley . New route: R033 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Platform allocation is now randomised at P0-2 & 4-5. 2022 26 June Sneak peek for Stepford Airport Central's overhaul was released. The sun sets on the next newly renovated station for another addition to #SneakPeekSundays 27 August - Version 1.10 Station overhauled. Now based on Gatwick Airport station . A lounge was added. The Signal Zone C signalling desk is now located at this station. Platform changes: Platform 0-2 still serves as the Stepford Connect terminating platforms, but now also allows through services to Airport Terminal 2 . Platform 3-6 still mainly serves AirLink , however Platform 3 is no longer limited to through services and Platforms 4 & 5 are no longer limited to terminating trains, allowing for through services as well. Platform 6 remains for through services from Airport Terminal 2 , but now also allows Stepford Connect and AirLink trains from that station and Farleigh Depot Road 11. Added Stepford Connect services to Airport Terminal 2 . New routes: R046 , R059 & R060 2023 2 April - Version 1.10.7 New route: R048 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added to Platform 3-6. Trivia [ ] The latest station model in Version 1.10 is based on Gatwick Airport station . This station is step-free. Stepford Airport Central is one of the few stations in SCR that has a Platform 0, and also one of the only stations that still have a Platform 0 since release. The only other stations (as of V2.0.1 ) to have a Platform 0 are Stepford Central and Llyn-by-the-Sea . The station looks much different with its second ( V1.0 ) and third ( V1.10 ) variant than it did prior to The Big Update . It had signs for what train arrived at the platform and it had a more futuristic design. This was one of the only few stations in the game that did not have a road near its entrance. The other stations with that trait at the time were Terminals 1 , 2 , 3 . This was changed in V1.10 , when the Airport Zone received an overhaul. Currently, the only station that does not have a road near its entrance is Airport Terminal 1 . This station is one of four multi-line through stations that are always stopped at by every route that approaches it, with the others being Stepford Central , Newry and Benton . Prior to the fix in V1.7 , in Stepford Connect 's map the name of this station was "Stepford Airport Central"; while in AirLink 's map it was just "Airport Central". This also happened to Stepford Airport Parkway . The user interface and the announcements also has this phenomenon, the user interface shows "Airport Central", while in the announcements , it is "Stepford Airport Central", for both station and onboard announcements. This also applies to other airport stops. Though this may be because the user interface cannot fit the whole station name, this is similar to Cambridge Street Parkway and Leighton Stepford Road where it is shown as ‚ÄúCambridge St Pkwy‚Äù and ‚ÄúLeighton Step Rd‚Äù respectively. Before the Five Million Update , Stepford Central was the hub of all AirLink services. This station is now considered to be the AirLink hub. Although AirLink was been rebranded, an old sign at the station, could have been seen at the end of Platform 4. In V1.8 , the sign was replaced with the rebranded signage. This station has the largest rectangle station sign on the entire network. This station has the largest National Rail logo in the entire network, located on the roof of the station. This station is the third station to have a lounge , following Stepford Central and Llyn-by-the-Sea . The AirLink tunnel portal outside the station leading to Airport Terminal 1 is called "Airport T1 Portal Access". ## Station 62: Stepford Airport Parkway

**Page ID:** 8677
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Stepford_Airport_Parkway

**Summary:**
Stepford Airport Parkway (commonly known as Airport Parkway ) is a through station located on the Airport Branch . Additionally, it is also a terminus for the AirLink Shuttle .

**Full Content:**

Stepford Airport Parkway Main Entrance Car Park Entrance Concourse Waiting Area Footbridge Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SAP C Station headcode Dispatching P Yes (2 slots) P1-2 , P3-5 Electrification Line Yes Airport Branch Station Information Location Farleigh District Zone Airport Zone Platforms 5 Tracks 5 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus ( Terminals Shuttle ) Benton Bridge 0.9 mi / 1.5 km Berrily 2.5 mi / 4.0 km (From BRY only) Elsemere Junction 3.1 mi / 5.0 km Leighton Stepford Road 4.7 mi / 7.6 km Stepford East 5.9 mi / 9.5 km Stepford Airport Central 0.6 mi / 1.0 km Preceding depot Following depot Airport Parkway Siding - Stepford Airport Parkway (commonly known as Airport Parkway ) is a through station located on the Airport Branch . Additionally, it is also a terminus for the AirLink Shuttle . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Stepford Airport Central and Airport Terminal 2 ; AirLink services to Stepford Central , Leighton Stepford Road , Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 and Airport Terminal 3 ; and AirLink Shuttle services to Airport Terminal 2 . This station provides an out of station interchange (OSI) with the nearby Airport West served and operated by Waterline . Trivia [ ] Before Version 1.10 : This station's entrance was based on Luton Airport Parkway 's entrance. This station had step-free access for interchange only. This was because all the platforms were connected with a sloped footbridge, while the path towards the entrance had a short flight of stairs in the way. This station had 216 parking spaces, behind Cambridge Street Parkway with 234. No AirLink trains to and from Leighton Stepford Road called at this station, passengers had to go there via Stepford Airport Central . After Version 1.10 : The whole station is based off Bristol Parkway in real life. There is a freight siding next to the station near Platform 5 (Stepford Airport Parkway Freight Sidings), this is also based on real life as there is a depot near Bristol Parkway. The station was moved closer to Airport West , with Airport West being northwest of Stepford Airport Parkway. Out of Station Interchange (OSI) between the aforementioned stations. The amount of parking spaces was increased to 1,013, beating Cambridge Street Parkway by 779. R056 was changed to stop here, making services to Leighton Stepford Road available. This is one of only five stations to have an elevator that serves more than two floors, the others being Stepford Central , Elsemere Junction , Ashlan Park and Rocket Parade . This station and Cambridge Street Parkway are the only stations in SCR to have "Parkway" in their names. Prior to V1.10 , this was the last AirLink station without step-free access to its entrance. This was also one of the two Stepford Connect stations that did not have wheelchair access to platforms. At that point, Water Newton was the only station that did not have wheelchair access to any of its platforms, before it finally became step-free in V2.0 . The sneak peek of Stepford Airport Parkway's overhaul was the last sneak peak to be posted by Managing Director Charlie_RBX on the #sneak-peeks channel on Discord. This station shares the headcode "P" with Port Benton . The only other pairs of stations that share a headcode are Leighton Stepford Road and Rayleigh Bay , which both share the "R" headcode and Benton and Barton , which both share the "B" headcode. ================================================================================

## Station 63: Stepford Central

**Page ID:** 14802
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Stepford_Central

**Summary:**
Stepford Central , formerly known as Stepford Town , is the major northern terminus of the Stepford Main Line , as well as a through station for services serving the Stepford Victoria Branch and Willowfield Branch .

**Full Content:**

Stepford Central Main Approach Entrance Airlink Side Entrance South Concourse Entrance Taxi Rank Entrance The Arches Entrance Airlink Side Interior South Concourse/The Arches Interior Taxi Rank Interior Underpass Main Ticket Hall Stepford Express ‚Äã Platforms Stepford Connect ‚Äã Platforms AirLink ‚Äã Platforms Waiting Area 1 Waiting Area 2 The Lounge Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform View 4 Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SCN A ( P0-15 ), J ( PA-D ) Station headcode Dispatching S Yes (4 slots) P0-9 , PA-D , P12-15 , P10-11 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Metro Core Section Station Information Location Stepford District Zone Stepford City Zone Platforms 16 ( CN , AL , EX ) 4 ( Metro ) Tracks 16 (mainline) 4 (underground) Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates & card readers Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus City Hospital 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Financial Quarter 0.8 mi / 1.3 km Beechley 0.7 mi / 1.1 km Stepford Victoria 1.5 mi / 2.4 km Stepford East 1.1 mi / 1.8 km St Helens Bridge 2.3 mi / 3.7 km Four Ways 0.6 mi / 1.0 km Benton 5.7 mi / 9.2 km Stepford Airport Central 7.4 mi / 11.9 km Elsemere Junction 3.9 mi / 6.3 km Leighton City 11.8 mi / 19.0 km Preceding depot Following depot Beechley Sidings Stepford Depot Stepford Central , formerly known as Stepford Town , is the major northern terminus of the Stepford Main Line , as well as a through station for services serving the Stepford Victoria Branch and Willowfield Branch . It is served by: Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Whitefield , Morganstown , Port Benton , Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 , Leighton City , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily , Morganstown , Barton and Port Benton ; AirLink services to Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 and Airport Terminal 3 ; and Stepford Express services to Benton , Leighton City , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea . There are 20 platforms at this station, all of which are in use, and 4 of which are deep-level, making it the largest station by platform count. The Stepford Rail Operations Centre is located in this station, which controls Zone A, Zone D and Zone G. Contents 1 Development history 2 Station layout 2.1 Legend 2.2 Exits 2.3 Legend 2.4 Priority 2.5 Entrance information 3 Platform lengths 4 Services 5 Station announcements 6 History 7 Trivia 8 Notes 9 Gallery Development history [ ] This station is one of the oldest stations in the game, as it was opened before The Big Update and continues to be the hub of Stepford Connect . The station was also AirLink 's hub, but later it was transferred to Stepford Airport Central in the Five Million Update due to the opening of the extension to Leighton Stepford Road . Prior to The Big Update , this station was known as Stepford Town . The new name was decided on by the players in a vote on the SCR Discord server. The other options were Stepford City, or to keep the name. Before Angel Pass was added, only Platforms 1-3 were used. After that, they were left vacant until Stepford Express came out in V1.4 and began using those platforms. This is the terminus of the Stepford Main Line. The line that goes beyond Stepford Central to Stepford Victoria is called the Stepford Victoria Branch and the line goes beyond Stepford Central to Willowfield is called the Willowfield Branch . Until V1.1 , only Platforms 4-7 were used, and it was a very quiet station as Stepford Depot did not exist, plus very few routes existed at that time. In addition, AirLink and Stepford Express were not released at the time. The concourse to Platform 11 was closed before V1.1 due to construction purposes, as well as no trains using that platform. Platforms 12 to 15 opened and were assigned to the newly-opened AirLink line which opened in V1.1 . As of the V1.4 update, all platforms at this station are in use. In the V1.4.1 update, this station got revamped with a shortened rainshed above Platforms 1-11. This station was lacking lights prior to this update. A siding near Platform 1 was added in V1.4.1 . It stayed unused for a long time until it finally became Platform 0 in V2.0.1 . In the V1.4.4 update, this station got a major revamp, made by yrrebRBLX, featuring a complete redesign which includes 3 new entrances (Taxi Rank, The Arches and South Concourse), management offices and the Stepford ROC . The default entrance became Approach Road. The station was reconstructed with a modular approach, which makes navigation around the station easier. Platform 11 and all AirLink platforms are secured by ticket barriers after this update. The Rail Operations Centre was relocated here. A first class AirLink lounge was also added but only completed in Version 1.7 , revealed in BanTech's revamped signalling video. Some original structures, like the Main Concourse seating area, remained after the update. The platform layout was unchanged, though they are now curved. In V2.0 , a new entrance for platforms 1-11 was added near the Taxi Rank, The Arches and South Concourse spawn points. However, this entrance was only accessible using stairs. In V2.0.1 , the unused siding was converted into platform 0 for terminating Stepford Express services. In V2.1 .3, a small part of the escalators to the Taxi Rank got removed and replaced by walls, and a new entrance also got added. You can't spawn there and it doesn't have a name yet. In V2.2 , 4 new platforms were introduced for Metro , being platforms A,B,C,D Station layout [ ] }} Click the arrow on the right to see the station layout. Entrance information [ ] For access to the Stepford Connect and Express Platforms 0-10, the best spawn point is the Main Approach. For access to the Stepford Connect (for Stepford Victoria , Beechley and Willowfield services) and AirLink Platforms 11-15, the best spawn point is AirLink Side. For access to Metro Platforms A-D, the best spawn point is the South Concourse. AirLink Side, South Concourse & The Arches entrances are linked together and meet below the AirLink concourse at the ground floor. Lifts are available at AirLink Side, South Concourse, The Arches and Taxi Rank. The Main Approach is step-free. For Signallers , Supervisors and Managers trying to access Stepford ROC , the only entrance is Main Approach. Platform lengths [ ] Note: these lengths are approximations. Platform 0 - 920 ft. Platform 0 & 1 have also been shortened slightly at the concourse end. 2025 1 January Sneak peek with a Metro Class 777 with Stepford Central as its destination was released. Wishing you a happy new year from everyone at SCR! Rail operations commencing early 2025. 1 April - Version 2.1.3 Metro construction barriers added at the South Concourse/The Arches entrance, under Platform 11. 11 May - Version 2.2 Metro concourse and platforms opened, adding Platforms A-D under the mainline platforms. New routes: R103 , R130 , R132 , R133 , R134 , R135 , R136 & R137 5 August - Version 2.2.1 A poster named "Bringing you closer" was added at Platform B-C. This won the first Community Spotlight hosted in May 2025. The poster 'Bringing you closer' and the creator cityuser is shown. Trivia [ ] This station was formerly based solely on Manchester Piccadilly , however after its renovation in V1.4.4, it is now also based on not only Manchester Piccadilly, but also London Waterloo (Platforms 12-15 are inspired by Waterloo's platforms 20-24). This station is one of eight stations in SCR operated by Transport for Stepford . This is the station with most entrances, at 5. Central Mall was the primary entrance until V1.4.4, when the Approach Road entrance was added and became the default entrance. As of Version 2.0 , Central Mall was demolished and made way for the new Main Approach. The original Approach Road entrance was renamed to the AirLink side. Prior to V1.9 , every Stepford Express route stopped at this station. Now, only 62% (or 8 out of 13) of routes stop here. [ note 1 ] The Concourses' locations are still similar to the old one, except for the South Concourse, which did not exist before V1.4.4. This is one of the stations which feature curved platforms. They were added in V1.4.4. Between V1.4.4 and V1.4.5, trains on Platforms 4-9 would shake if they were departing and another train arrived at the station. At the old Central Mall entrance, players could see the mall and a square located right before it. And at the Taxi Rank entrance, there are bays for taxis. This scenery really makes any passengers going into the station feel like they are actually in a city. At the Taxi Rank entrance, there is a large, brown-brick building labelled as Great Stepford Railway. This could be a former name for Transport for Stepford . The SCR Headquarters was relocated a bit away from this station in V1.4.4 to allow more space for the station building which was made bigger. Qualified Driver Trainings were formerly conducted here, before being relocated to Stepford East ROC during V1.1 . However, after Version 1.4.4, they were relocated back to be held here at an entrance point (more specifically, Central Mall ). Since V1.10.4, these trainings are now held in a separate purpose-built training map. Managers ' and Directors ' Offices are located here as of V1.4.4. Most of them are inside the Management Office above the AirLink Concourse at the south end of the station, while the office for Innovations Director is opposite, which is located at the north end of the station, next to Stepford ROC , and the office of Signaller Manager and Operations Manager are on the right side of the ROC, while Community Director and Operations Director offices are on the left side of the ROC. This was the first station in SCR to have a lounge . The other stations that have a lounge are Airport Central , Northshore , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-sea . The '???' feature on the former roadmap was accidentally removed when the station was upgraded, leading some to believe that that was the secret update, as there was no announcement about it. The '???' ultimately turned out to be the introduction of the new role, Guards , in V1.5 . Trains from Stepford Depot can go to almost all 16 platforms at this station. Platform 10 cannot be accessed from the depot as it is an eastbound only platform. It is faster to walk than taking a train from here to Stepford Victoria . Another major station, Morganstown , has all 5 operators serving it but having 9 less (or twice as less) platforms than Stepford Central (if counting Platform 5A and 5B as seperate platforms). This station is one of four multi-line through stations that are always stopped at by every route that approaches it, with the others being Newry , Stepford Airport Central and Benton . This is one of two stations to have a set of two elevators, the other one being at Airport Central , on platforms 5 and 6. When going to Platforms 0-10 from Airlink Side, or vice versa, the player actually passes through ticket barriers three times. Despite being the largest station in the game, Stepford Central is not a junction station. As of Version 2.0.1, this is one of three stations to have a Platform 0, the others being Airport Central and Llyn by the Sea . In very early versions of the game, there was what appeared to be a Class 390 stationary on the ground beside the station, as found at 4:35 in the YouTube video, " Stepford County Railway: Benton - Stepford Town (Oldest recorded SCR gameplay) ". The train in question This station has entrance with bike racks near the Main Approach Entrance. SECRET BADGE 1 There is an Easter Egg at this station. Spawn as a passenger at the Main Approach Entrance of this station, then go down to Stece_Sama statue and walk to the arches. There is a narrow way between a wall and the bridge. Players can see a 9-¬æ sign at the end. They can pass through the wall of the bridge where it's attached. After passing through it, the player can see a huge empty room and a wall with the text "An easter egg? But it's not easter yet! I guess BanTech just likes to mess around. Welcome to the big empty space under Stepford Central! Touch me for a free badge". When they touch the wall, they will get the badge "I wonder what's in here...", and the text on the wall will change to "Hehe, that tickles" SECRET BADGE 2 Players can get another badge after spawning at South Concourse and walking to the statue of a person holding a globe. If a player climbs the statue, they will get the The Weight of the World badge . The person has a teapot on his head because the person is yrrebRBLX (a former Product Developer ). ## Station 64: Stepford East

**Page ID:** 4713
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Stepford_East

**Summary:**
Stepford East is an elevated major through station on the Stepford Main Line .

**Full Content:**

This won the first Community Spotlight hosted in May 2025. 'Your new operator' by bnincl Trivia [ ] This station is based on London Bridge Station in London, UK . A new depot was built next to this station in V1.1 . It is used by Stepford Connect and AirLink (and later Stepford Express ). The old Stepford East Rail Operations Centre was located next to this station. It was attached to the station, and the entrance to the building was at the High Street entrance. It was moved to Stepford Central in Version 1.4.4 Signallers could have still entered the old ROC as the barriers were still working. It was eventually removed in V1.6 and replaced by a tall building. The entrance at High Street was sealed off. This station is one of four station which are operated by Transport for Stepford , as they are located within the Stepford District. The others are Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central and St Helens Bridge . It is also the only Transport for Stepford station that has no terminating platforms. This is one of the most popular dispatching stations due to the fact that one Dispatcher can dispatch all the Stepford Connect trains that stop here. However, there is typically no AirLink Dispatcher unless AirLink is being " flooded ". Upon the release of V1.4 , as Stepford Express does not stop here, the popularity decreased and transferred to St Helens Bridge as both Stepford Connect and Stepford Express can be dispatched at St Helens Bridge . It is still common to find Dispatchers at Stepford East's Stepford Connect platforms though. This station is also a very popular station for passengers as it is one of the busiest stations in the game, as well as it being a good place to trainspot passing Stepford Express services and trains coming out of the nearby Stepford Depot . Additionally, the frequent appearance of a Dispatcher here makes it a more social station. There was at one point a bug that would cause Dispatchers to be flung by departing trains, requiring Dispatchers to respawn. This is caused by the quirks ROBLOX physics engine, and is no longer possible due the updated train movement system. Due to a good network of roads in the area, it is possible to walk to all stations in Stepford City and even Elsemere Pond . However, it is impossible to walk to Elsemere Junction or Whitefield Lido from here. Before V1.6 , it was impossible to walk to Stepford Central from here. This station is the largest through-only station on the network. This station was the first in the game to have a >7 car stop marker . There are 6-7 car Stop Markers on the Stepford Connect platforms, and further S Stop Marker , though no train used the former until the Class 717 with 6 cars was released in Version 1.8.2 . In Version 2.2 , however, all Class 717 units were transferred to Metro operator, once again leaving them unused. The S Stop Markers still remain unused, unless a player overshoots the correct stop marker. In V1.8 , 7-8 car stop markers were added to AirLink platforms, hinting future 7 and 8 coach trains on AirLink . In V2.1 , these were used by the double Class 387 . Stepford East was the only station to have 8 car stop markers in the network until V1.10 , when they were also added to Stepford Airport Parkway and Stepford Airport Central . ## Station 65: Stepford High Street

**Page ID:** 3228
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Stepford_High_Street

**Summary:**
Stepford High Street (colloquially called High Street ) is a through station located in the Metro Core Section . It is named after the street the station is located at.

**Full Content:**

Stepford High Street Bus Station Entrance South Side Entrance Concourse Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Disused Connect Platform Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SHS J Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) PA-D Electrification Line Yes Metro Core Section Station Information Location Stepford District Zone Stepford City Zone Platforms 4 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via ramp Ticket machines No Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Stepford East 0.6 mi / 1.0 km Whitefield Lido 0.4 mi / 0.6 km St Helens Bridge 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Track Layout to Whitefield Lido High Street to Stepford East Stepford High Street (colloquially called High Street ) is a through station located in the Metro Core Section . It is named after the street the station is located at. This station is served by Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , Stepford United Football Club , Barton , Berrily , Morganstown and Port Benton . History [ ] 2019 28 April - Version 1.2 Stepford High Street added to the network as part of the Whitefield extension , as a Stepford Connect through station with a very curved island platform. New routes: R020 , R021 , R022 & R023 22 February - Version 1.4.1 Added OFF indicators and Stepford Connect signs. Removed the Metro red. 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Station overhauled. Concourse now consists of glass walls with concourse information boards and seating added to the station. New route: R031 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Added OHLE. Route change: R022 ( Stepford Victoria ‚Üí Beechley <> Whitefield ) Now terminates at Beechley. No longer stops at Stepford Victoria , Financial Quarter , City Hospital , Whitefield Lido & Houghton Rake . 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Additional OFF indicators have been added for better visibility. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Stepford High Street is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect no longer serves this station. New Metro platforms opened underground, but the elevated platform has been abandoned. Route removals: R020 , R022 No longer stops here. New routes: R002 , R006 , R008 , R027 , R030 , R034 , R130 , R132 , R133 , R135 , R136 & R137 Trivia [ ] This station before Version 2.2, served as a landmark for trainspotters, as it is said to give the perfect passer-by view of the Stepford Main Line 's diverse traction. This station used to have no mark on the Network Map . Prior to Version 2.2 , this station was jokingly referred to as the "90 degree station" due to its platforms curving 90¬∞. Some players used to report lag issues at the station, likely because of the 90 degree curve and many parts were overlapping into each other, causing z-fighting , which in turn, causes lag. Because of the curve, the station had very big gaps (at some places) between trains and the platform. Many Dispatchers and Guards disliked the station because the sharp curve makes it difficult to easily complete the procedure. The strange placement of OFF indicators does not help this. The curved platform of this station was similar to Platforms 5 and 6 at Ebbsfleet International station on High Speed 1. As of Version 2.2 , The platforms A and B are still curved 90¬∞ since they serve services to/from Stepford United Football Club . Due to this, Dispatchers were able to dispatch a train on an adjacent platform (i.e. Dispatching the train on Platform 1 on Platform 2), as this improves visibility for dispatching on curved platforms. This station has step-free access. This station used to be elevated when it was managed by Stepford Connect . The elevated platform is now abandoned with the entrance blocked off and the new underground entrance placed right behind the old one. The Connect station sign was replaced to "Do not alight here". It is the only station sign to be self-illuminated as typical station sign would be illuminated using street light. Players can still access the abandoned platforms via trespassing. Stepford High Street Shopping Centre is located just west of the station. This station offers access to the High Street Metro Signalling Centre and Stepford High Street Head Office. Oddly enough, this station used to have no ticket machines. Players can walk from this station to Stepford East and St Helens Bridge without trespassing. This station is one of the two stations to not have a sign with its name in the entire network , alongside Four Ways . Notes [ ] ‚Üë This announcement was used in-game before the introduction of Metro , however, is no longer used. Gallery [ ] Prior to Version 1.6 [ ] The station before its official release (players can see legacy station signs). The station before its official release. ## Station 66: Stepford Southgate

**Page ID:** 17902
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Stepford_Southgate

**Summary:**
Cancelled feature

**Full Content:**

Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Stepford Southgate Operational Information Served by Managed by Metro Metro (Presumably) Station code SSO Station Information Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Service Information Preceding station Following station St Helens South University Stepford Southgate was a proposed station to be part of Metro and High Speed. However, due to the cancellation of both operators, the station was demolished in The Big Update . Return speculation [ ] With Metro 's return in Version 2.2 , many players speculated that the original Metro Loop could return along with the previously proposed stations. However, the Metro Loop did not return and a new loop including Coxly Newtown was added instead. It is unknown if an introduction of the Metro Loop is planned in the future. Trivia [ ] This station was part of the Metro Loop , which has also been demolished within The Big Update except Stepford Victoria and Beechley ( Financial Quarter ), which became the Stepford Victoria Branch . Prior to The Big Update , Stepford Southgate was never actually completed. If the player was to go there in the Legacy Version of Stepford County Railway , they would find an empty platform between St Helens South and University . Notes [ ]

## Station 67: Stepford United Football Club

**Page ID:** 9055
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Stepford_United_Football_Club

**Summary:**
Stepford United Football Club , or simply Stepford UFC , is a through station and terminus midway through the Whitefield Branch .

**Full Content:**

Stepford UFC Main Entrance Stadium Car Park Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone UFC A Station headcode Dispatching U Yes (1 slot) P1-4 Electrification Line Yes Whitefield Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Zone Stepford City Zone Platforms 4 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via ramps Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Stepford East 1.4 mi / 2.3 km Whitefield Lido 0.6 mi / 1.0 km Terminus Woodhead Lane 1.2 mi / 1.9 km Track Layout to Woodhead Lane TMD to Whitefield Lido Stepford United Football Club , or simply Stepford UFC , is a through station and terminus midway through the Whitefield Branch . It serves Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Central and Whitefield ; and Metro services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria and Stepford Central . This station was opened in Version 1.2 and received multiple facelifts before its eventual overhauls in Version 1.6 and Version 1.8 . It was the north-eastern edge of the former Stepford City Zone . To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2019 24 February Sneak peek for Stepford UFC was released. Here we are again! This is my second contribution to the SCR Dev Team! This next station is a little bigger than my last one but here it is. üòÅ 28 April - Version 1.2 Stepford United Football Club added to the network as part of the Whitefield extension , as a Stepford Connect through station as well as a terminus, serving a football stadium. Resembles Darlington Station . Platform 1 & 4 are through platforms while Platform 2 & 3 are bay platforms. Dispatcher and Guard trainings are held here. New routes: R020 , R021 , R022 & R023 2020 1 May - Version 1.5 Dispatcher trainings are no longer held here. Now held at Faymere . Guard trainings are now held here. However later moved to Faymere as well. 22 June - Version 1.6 Station overhauled. New roof design, but the overall structure remains the same, with some colour changes. Guard trainings are now held here again. Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New route: R031 20 August - Version 1.6.5 Dispatcher trainings are now held here again. 2021 7 July - Version 1.7.4 Dispatcher trainings are no longer held here. Now at held Willowfield . 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled. Roof has been removed. No longer resembles Darlington Station . Platform 1 & 2 are now bay platforms and Platform 3 & 4 are now through platforms. New training briefing centre added next to the station. Dispatcher trainings are now held here again. Added OHLE. Platform allocation is now randomised at P1-2. Route change: R022 ( Stepford Victoria ‚Üí Beechley <> Whitefield ) Now terminates at Beechley. No longer stops at Stepford Victoria , Financial Quarter , City Hospital , Whitefield Lido & Houghton Rake . 2023 6 March - Version 1.10.4 Dispatcher and Guard trainings are no longer held here with the new training map. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Stepford UFC is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect no longer terminates here. New route: R103 Trivia [ ] Before V1.6 , this station used to resemble Darlington Station in Darlington, UK. There is a football stadium outside the station. This was made by former Signaller Manager billythepet . Before V1.8 , the stadium was to the west of the station. After it, the stadium and car-park were moved to the east of the station. After the overhaul in V1.8 , this station has been disliked by some of the community, due to the station looking more generic and the unique roof being removed. Before V1.4.4, this station resembled the old Stepford Central , but was significantly smaller, and only had 4 platforms instead of 15. Before trespassers found this station before Version 1.2 was officially released, many players presumed this station, and others previewed, were along the Llyn-by-the-Sea extension. Pre-season matches occurred for a big season after the release of this station. As a result, Stepford UFC merch was previewed in the SCR Official Discord. This was the first station to be near a stadium. And along with Millcastle Racecourse , they are the only stations to have a stadium nearby. The stadium at Millcastle Racecourse is the only one to not be purposed for football games, being purposed for horse racing instead. This station had an advertisement for Waterline that was unique to it. It featured Eden Quay . It was removed in V1.4.6. A remade version of the advertisement was added in V1.7.1. The new version of the advertisement is no longer exclusive to Stepford UFC. This station used to be two wide staircases leading up to two bay platforms with two underpasses between them in SCR Legacy . Pedestrian routes to Whitefield Lido and Woodhead Lane are made possible by a road that runs parallel to the tracks. This station has the longest station name when fully extended with 29 characters. The longest single word station names are Westercoast , Willowfield and Morganstown , with 11 characters. Stepford UFC has 12 characters when condensed. Dispatcher and Guard trainings once took place here. After V1.8 , the sign at the end of the terminating tracks that said "Welcome to Stepford United Football Club" was removed. A similar sign can still be found at the Willowfield station exit. There is a rusty lamp post lying in the bushes between Platforms 2 and 3. According to former Product Developer Mattyx2013 , some angry football fans "threw it out". To the west of the station, there are some strange cut-out grey baseplates forming a circle. These are supposedly from the pre- V1.8 Stepford UFC station. One of these supposed roads even connects to Hemdon Park . One of the signs of this station is floating above the platform. This station is often nicknamed as "Stepford KFC", a spinoff based on its similar spelling with the global fried chicken fast food chain KFC. ## Station 68: Stepford Victoria

**Page ID:** 475
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Stepford_Victoria

**Summary:**
Stepford Victoria is the terminus of the Stepford Victoria Branch .

**Full Content:**

Stepford Victoria Spawn Entrance Ticket Office Shops Concourse Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone SVC/SCV A Station headcode Dispatching V Yes (1 slot) P1-6 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Victoria Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Zone Stepford City Zone Platforms 6 Tracks 6 Accessibility Step-free access via ramp Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus Financial Quarter 0.6 mi / 1.0 km City Hospital 0.7 mi / 1.1 km Stepford Central 1.5 mi / 2.4 km Preceding depot Following depot - Beechley Sidings Track Layout to Financial Quarter Stepford Victoria is the terminus of the Stepford Victoria Branch . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Stepford Airport Central , Airport Terminal 2 , Leighton City , Edgemead and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Metro services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily , Morganstown , Barton and Port Benton . In Version 1.10.4 , the station received a minor revamp that extended the centre platforms and added extra lighting to the platforms, as well as a ticket office and a shopping area below platform level. New routes: R136 & R137 Trivia [ ] The station resembles London Charing Cross , but the entrance to the station is very different to its real life counterpart. This station has step-free access. This station opened in V1.1 , which was released on the 31st of December 2018. This station is operated by Transport for Stepford . Along with most stations located near Stepford, where most Stepford Connect stations co-operate with Transport for Stepford . The other 7 stations which are also operated by Transport for Stepford are Stepford Central , Stepford East , St Helens Bridge , Morganstown , Benton , Leighton City and Llyn-by-the-Sea . Originally, this station was going to serve an operator called High Speed, which would have used a line adjacent to the Stepford Main Line to get onto the Morganstown Branch , where trains would have then used the then-unused southern section of a triangle junction at Morganstown to get back onto the Stepford Main Line . However, plans changed and the original route was demolished. The station was also planned to be on the Metro Loop , which was cancelled. The station was completely rebuilt in V1.1 , and the Tramlink stop adjacent to the station had to be demolished to make way for the new concourse. It is most common to see the free Class 357 and Class 717 trains here due to the Stepford Victoria to Stepford Airport Central ( R005 ), Stepford United Football Club ( R023 ) and Leighton City ( R045 ) routes starting here, as they are the free starter routes. Prior to V1.4 , this station had purple information boards, which made people think that Stepford Express would serve here. Prior to V1.6 , this station had no seats and ticket barriers. Despite this station having more platforms than average, it is rare for more than three of them to be occupied at once. This station lacks in detail with little to no scenery near the station. This station is exactly parallel to Stepford Central and can be seen from Stepford Central with a high enough render distance and vice-versa. Prior to V1.8 , there was a "secret" route to Llyn-by-the-Sea that was not shown on the line map that starts at Stepford Victoria. It was R026 , in which the occurrence of the route was rare as it is exclusive to the Class 68 , the most expensive train in SCR that not many people own. As of V1.8 , the route is now shown on the Stepford Connect map (Regional 1). Class 444 now shares the route with the Class 68 . Getting to Stepford Central is quicker on foot than by train. It takes 1.5 minutes on foot and a minimum of 2 minutes by train (this is worsened by the Beechley Triangle often being congested). Prior to V1.10.4, this station lacked ticket machines despite being a large station. Inside the station facade are a row of inaccessible doors, which some believed led to signalling offices like at other stations such as Stepford Central . The platforms 5 and 6 of this station are wider, the cause is unknown. This station was originally made by former manager AMAViation, who has since left. Prior to British Railway's (Roblox) 1.1.0 update, one of the station signs on Victoria Harbour (Platform 1) read "Stepford Victoria". This was a reference to this station. [ note 1 ] The sign was removed after the update. Notes [ ] ‚Üë British Railway Wiki : Victoria Harbour (Trivia) "Prior to 1.1.0, one of the station signs on Platform 1 read "Stepford Victoria". This was a reference to the Stepford Victoria station in Stepford County Railway, another Roblox train game." ## Station 69: University

**Page ID:** 18100
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/University

**Summary:**
Cancelled feature

**Full Content:**

Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. Cancelled feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed, but was ultimately not released to the main game. These are considered cancelled features. University Operational Information Served by Managed by Metro (Proposed) Metro Station code UNI Station Information Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Service Information Preceding station Following station Stepford Southgate Stepford Victoria University was a proposed station to be part of Metro . However, due to the cancellation of Metro, the station was demolished in The Big Update . Return speculation [ ] With Metro 's return in Version 2.2 , many players speculated that the original Metro Loop could return along with the previously proposed stations. However, the Metro Loop did not return and a new loop including Coxly Newtown was added instead. It is unknown if an introduction of the Metro Loop is planned in the future. Trivia [ ] This station was part of the former Metro Loop , which was also demolished in The Big Update except Stepford Victoria and Willowfield ( Financial Quarter ), which became the Stepford Victoria Branch.

**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Upper_Staploe

**Summary:**
Upper Staploe is a limited-service through station on the Stepford Main Line that opened in Version 1.7 .

**Full Content:**

This page is about the Stepford Connect station. For the unused Metro station, see Upper Staploe (Metro) . To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2020 27 September Sneak peek for Upper Staploe was released. Couldn't really do up this line without giving the people of this village their rail service back, could I... ü§î 29 October - Version 1.7 Upper Staploe added to the network, located between Hampton Hargate and Water Newton , as a limited-service Stepford Connect through station with 2 side platforms. New route: R039 2021 5 December - Version 1.8 Added Stepford Connect services to Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Leighton West and Westwyvern . New routes: R003 , R025 & R044 Route change: R039 ( Benton <> Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City ) Now terminates at Leighton City. 2022 27 February - Version 1.8.2 Added Stepford Connect services to the Stepford Victoria branch . New route: R045 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 CIS Boards and benches added. 2025 5 August - Version 2.2.1 A poster named "Enjoy Metro" was added near the station. This won the first Community Spotlight hosted in May 2025. Enjoy Metro' by Yengamertv Trivia [ ] This station has step-free access. This station was sneak peeked by Charlie_RBX on 27 September 2020. Upper Staploe's sneak peek It was not known that the slow tracks slightly diverge off the mainline to serve this station. The fast tracks are around 250 metres from here. Before V1.8 , R039 was the only route that stopped here, which once made it the least served on the Stepford Connect network. This station used to be the only one that did not have any CIS Boards and benches until V2.0 . Before V1.8 , this station was one of the two only stations served by Stepford Connect which do not have a route calling at Stepford Central , along with Millcastle Racecourse . It was also the only station on the entire Stepford Connect network at that time for not having a train going to any stations in Stepford City without interchange . After the aforementioned update, the addition of R003 and R025 calling at this station provides direct services to the Stepford City Centre from here, with the trait transferred to Leighton West . The announcements for Platform 1 are known to play too early before the train arrives. This is likely due to the placement of the sensor much further away from the station. The same occurs for Platform 1 at New Harrow . The chat filter censors Upper Staploe to "##### #taploe", likely because the Roblox chat filter interpreting it as an attempt to say the word "Uppers", a slang term for a type of illegal drug. There is a road connecting Farleigh to this station, this also means Upper Staploe is quite near the Stepford Airport . If one walked from this station to Farleigh , it would be faster than taking a train. Before Farleigh was added in V1.10 , this road used to lead out of Upper Staploe before floating above the baseplate without supports and then abruptly stopping in the middle of nowhere. The Staploe Tap Just outside the station, there is a Commercial Building named "The Staploe Tap", which is likely to be a pub. ## Station 71: Upper Staploe (Metro)

**Page ID:** 19016
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Upper_Staploe_(Metro)

**Summary:**
Unused feature

**Full Content:**

Unused feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed and added to the game, but ultimately left unused. Unused feature This article or section covers content that was once proposed and added to the game, but ultimately left unused. This page is about the unused Metro station. For the Stepford Connect station, see Upper Staploe . Upper Staploe Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by (proposed) Station code Signal zone USL D Station Information Platforms 2 (0 in service) Tracks 4 (2 in service) Service Information Preceding station Following station Hampton Hargate Water Newton Upper Staploe is an abandoned through station formerly proposed to be served by Metro . Contents 1 Track layout 1.1 Legend 2 Trivia 3 Gallery Track layout [ ] G Tracks (Platform 1) == Abandoned Metro tracks == Abandoned Metro tracks ‚Üí AirLink & Stepford Express towards Water Newton (Passing) ‚Üê AirLink & Stepford Express towards Hampton Hargate (Passing) (Platform 2) Legend [ ] ‚Üí Eastbound ‚Üê Westbound == Tracks Trivia [ ] The station before V2.0 added the abandoned tracks This station was supposed to be served by Metro , but became abandoned when Metro was scrapped after The Big Update . This station is one of two abandoned stations in the game that are still intact currently, with the other being Robinson Way , an abandoned Tramlink station. Before V1.7 , the platforms were arranged in a way that each of the two platforms were served by a different operator. The platform towards Llyn-by-the-Sea was located on the Stepford Connect tracks, while the platform towards Stepford City was (and still is) located on the AirLink / Stepford Express tracks. This is the only planned Metro station that is just left abandoned in game, as Coxly Newtown was reopened in V2.2 . Diagram of the track layout This station still remains in the game as of V2.2 , with the AirLink / Stepford Express tracks passing through. The station along with the area around it was redesigned in V2.0 , extending the village and adding overgrown tracks on the Leighton -bound platform. This made it so that the station is accessible from the Stepford Connect Upper Staploe station to here without trespassing . Going past the wooden barriers is still considered trespassing. Water Newton is a through station on the Stepford Main Line .

It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Benton , Leighton City , Leighton West , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and limited AirLink services to Airport Terminal 3 and Leighton Stepford Road . There's always more to see... üóëÔ∏èüöÜ 12 August - Version 2.0 Station upgraded, with footbridge access to Platform 3 and 4, and addition of lifts. New route: R057 Water Newton is now dispatchable. 12 September - Version 2.0.1 Class 80x stop marker added to Platform 3. Trivia [ ] The station is based on Pitsea station in Essex. Before V2.0 , the station was not step-free due to its lack of lifts or accessible ramps. It was also the last station in the game to not have step free access of any kind. Water Newton is one of 10 stations that got an upgrade in V1.7 . [ 1 ] Prior to this upgrade, a section of track near this station had a terminating junction. Prior to The Big Update , this station had no entrance and was very under-detailed. Despite considerable investment in enhancing it, the station still remains uninterested in by passengers and drivers alike. In The Big Update , one of the two island platforms was demolished, with the singular remaining one still being used. Despite this station being called "Water Newton", there are no bodies of water near this station. It is possible to walk to Rosedale Village from here via road without trespassing within a few minutes. The AWS ramp in question Oddly, there was a random AWS ramp hidden in the bushes near Platform 1, although it has since been removed. Prior to V2.0 , players could not access Platform 4 from the rest of the station, unless the player trespassed or walked from the road behind. In V2.0 , a new special sign was added at the entrance, displaying "Welcome to Water Newton", unlike the regular station sign, which simply shows the station name. This is the only Stepford Connect managed station that is served by AirLink . ## Station 73: West Benton

**Page ID:** 4931
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/West_Benton

**Summary:**
West Benton is a through station on the Newry Branch .

**Full Content:**

West Benton Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Station View Viewing Area Matty Statue Pet Supplies 165/0 Exhibition Model Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone WBN F Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Newry Branch Station Information Location Benton District Zone Benton Zone Platforms 2 Tracks 6 Accessibility Step-free access via ramp Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Faraday Road 0.4 miles / 644 metres Benton 0.42 miles / 676 metres West Benton is a through station on the Newry Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Newry Harbour , Newry , Connolly , Airport Terminal 2 , Farleigh , Esterfield , Morganstown and Greenslade . This station was upgraded in Version 1.9.1, along with Ashlan Park . Route change: R014 ( Newry <> James Street ‚Üí Esterfield ) Now terminates at Esterfield. New routes: R017 & R018 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 New route: R120 Trivia [ ] This is former Product Developer Mattyx2013 's favourite station. He is also fond of Starryloch . The station loosely resembles Heaton station in Newcastle. They have a similar layout and similar features. However, the modern features make West Benton also similar to Pelaw metro station along the Tyne and Wear metro line. This is one of the greatest places for trainspotting, as Stepford Connect and Stepford Express trains can often be seen passing right next to this station. Some inexperienced drivers tend to skip West Benton as they drive faster than the speed limit and do not realise how close West Benton is to Faraday Road and Benton . It is speculated that West Benton Skips Co , a commercial building in Westercoast , is a reference to this fact. Before V1.1.7, West Benton was not a dispatchable station. When it was made one, however, former Product Developer Mattyx2013 was reportedly dispatching there the moment the change was made. West Benton Pet Supplies, a commercial building , is located just around the curve from this station. Strangely, the V1.9.1 upgrade added another "Supplies" to the building signage. It is unknown whether this was made on purpose. A viewing deck has been added beside the station entrance in V1.4.1 . This station has step-free access. The speed limit between here to Benton was 75 MPH. It was changed to 45 MPH to Benton in V1.4.1 and from Benton in V1.6 , and reverted back to 75 MPH from Benton in V1.7 . The speed limit through this station going to Benton is 50 MPH as of V1.9 . West Benton is one of the few stations where players are allowed to speed up when approaching it, as the speed limit raises from 30 to 75 MPH shortly before the station, from Benton . This station's name is censored in game chat for no apparent reason. The players name West Benton in a fun way: Best Wenton. This happens to Beaulieu Park , Coxly , Whitney Green , Connolly and Upper Staploe , too. Beechley is also censored, but it has a clearer explanation. Players can walk from here to Benton , Coxly and Faraday Road without trespassing . The stop marker for Platform 1 was hidden behind a wall and could not be seen from outside. This is due to the straightening of the wall adjacent to the station. Prior to V1.7 , this wall had a slight inclination with the marker peeking from the side. This has been pointed out by many including on the Discord #screenshots channel. The stop marker has now been moved onto the platform in V1.7.2. With the station upgrade in V1.9.1, a model of the Class 165/0 was added on a exhibition stand, that labels the following text in the top right corner of the stand "This is one of the old models of the old NGv2 trains created by Mattyx2013 (statue outside)" Prior to Version 2.0 , " models " was misspelt as " modals ". This station, along with Ashlan Park 's upgrade was not sneak peeked before V1.9.1's release. There is a graffiti outside the small park behind Mattyx2013 's statue that says " Matty wuz also 'Ere ", similar in style to the one seen at Whitefield . According to Mattyx2013 , there were two initial overhaul versions of the station for V1.9.1, with the final design merging features from the two. [ 1 ] The first version was reminiscent of the former model of the station, albeit with some changes. However the file for the station inadvertently vanished. The second version was based off a park-like metro station, however this received disapproval from former (then-incumbent) Managing Director Charlie_RBX . West Benton is notable for being in the middle of Faraday Road TMD and Benton Siding , with both spawn points facing away from the station. This makes it difficult to reach the station easily from a depot , with Esterfield Mainline Depot being the only one to do so. Gallery [ ] Scenery around the station before V1.4.1 Scenery around the entrance before Benton's revamp in V1.7 Pre-V1.9.1 Entrance Pre-V1.9.1 Stairs Pre-V1.9.1 Platforms A graffiti that reads "Matty Wuz Also 'Ere" located just beside Mattyx2013 's statue. This graffiti is painted in a similar fashion to the one seen at Whitefield References [ ] ‚Üë Mattyx2013 (25 June 2022). "The Secret Versions of West Benton" . Retrieved 30 June 2022 via YouTube. ## Station 75: Westercoast

**Page ID:** 5585
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Westercoast

**Summary:**
Westercoast is a through station on the Stepford Main Line that opened in Version 1.4 .

**Full Content:**

Westercoast Main Entrance Platform 1 Entrance Interior Station Forecourt Entrance Interior Footbridge Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Town Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone WST E Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Llyn District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via ramps Ticket machines Yes & ticket office available Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Faymere 1.27 miles / 2.04 kilometres Edgemead 2.06 miles / 3.31 kilometres Leighton City 3.69 miles / 5.94 kilometres Millcastle Racecourse 0.84 miles / 1.35 kilometres Millcastle 1.2 miles / 1.93 kilometres Northshore 4.80 miles / 7.72 kilometers Llyn-by-the-Sea 5.76 miles / 9.27 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot Faymere Green SB Depot - Track Layout to Millcastle Racecourse Westercoast Viaduct to Faymere Green TMD Westercoast is a through station on the Stepford Main Line that opened in Version 1.4 . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Leighton City , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and limited Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry and Llyn-by-the-Sea . New routes: R050 & R102 24 December - Version 2.1 New route: R088 Trivia [ ] The section of track near this station is similar to a real life station on the East Coast Mainline named Welwyn North . (From London/Stepford). Similarities include the 4 track sections from both sides narrowing to 2 tracks, approaching the station. The viaduct and subsequent tunnel is also done in a similar fashion to in real life. This station and its scenery were built by Product Developer thehazad9. Dispatcher trainings used to take place here from V1.5 to V1.6.5; the previous location was at Stepford United Football Club , along with Faymere . They moved back to Stepford United Football Club in V1.6.5, then moved to Willowfield for a while in V1.7.4, and subsequently back to Stepford United Football Club again in V1.8 . Although this station is dispatchable, it is very rare to see a dispatcher here as it is rare to see Stepford Connect trains venture past Leighton City (as it is a terminus for the free route R045 ). The line that this station is situated on is served by Stepford Express services, however none of them stopped here until R083 was introduced in V1.9. This station is considered to have some of the best scenery in the game, with more Commercial Buildings than any other station lining the town's streets. There are more Commercial Buildings containing the word " Bodin " (4) in this stations' scenery than "Westercoast" (2). The largest viaduct in Stepford County is found at Westercoast ( Westercoast Viaduct ). The part of the viaduct in the town has ‚ÄúWestercoast‚Äù written in golden letters on its side. Westercoast was the first station on the Llyn extension to be officially sneak-peeked. This station, as well as Morganstown and Willowfield , are the longest single-word station names, with the overall longest station name being Stepford United Football Club . This station, along with Whitefield , had large "Welcome to (Station Name)" signs outside prior to Version 1.6 . They were replaced with plain platform signs. This station is still quite unique with its "Services To: Llyn-By-The-Sea" and "Services To: Stepford/Leighton" signs at the entrances to both platforms. The plain platform signs was removed in V1.8 . Prior to V1.8.4, there was only a foot crossing between the platforms. It is sometimes hard to get to Platform 1 because Westercoast only has two spawns on the westbound side and the crossing sometimes despawns you as the tracks here are more leveled up than other foot crossings in SCR. As of V1.8.4, this can be circumvented by using the footbridge. When arriving this station from Faymere , the driver would always be 1‚Äì2 minutes early unless the train was already delayed before reaching Faymere , as the timing between the stations was set too high. This can cause SPADs for fast Stepford Express trains which do not stop at this station. Additionally, Stepford Express trains can also be delayed if they are being held up by a Stepford Connect train at this station. This station received a minor upgrade in V1.8 , adding a concourse and small buildings on both sides, however it was not mentioned in the official patch notes. This was likely accidental. This station has the National Rail Double Arrow symbol on the east entrance station sign. It can also be found at Stepford Airport Central , Rosedale Village and Northshore . On 24 April 2022, a sneak peek showing the addition of a footbridge to the station was revealed, being released into V1.8.4 the next day. The footbridge received criticism quickly, with players stating that it does not fit the station, as well as being unnecessary. Oddly, despite having a Llyn via Benton Stepford Express route ( R088 ) stopping here, the Stepford Express map does not include this station on said line. ## Station 76: Westwyvern

**Page ID:** 6857
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Westwyvern

**Summary:**
Westwyvern is a major through station on the Stepford Main Line , with some services terminating here.

**Full Content:**

Westwyvern Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Platform View 4 Waiting Room The Lounge Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone WYV E Station headcode Dispatching W Yes (1 slot) P1-4 Electrification Line Yes Stepford Main Line Station Information Location Llyn District Zone - Platforms 4 Tracks 4 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Millcastle 2.2 mi / 3.5 km Edgemead 5.6 mi / 9.0 km Leighton City 7.3 mi / 11.8 km Terminus Starryloch 1.4 mi / 2.3 km Northshore 2.1 mi / 3.4 km Llyn-by-the-Sea 3.8 mi / 6.1 km Preceding depot Following depot Faymere Green SB Depot - Westwyvern is a major through station on the Stepford Main Line , with some services terminating here. It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central , St Helens Bridge , Leighton City , Leighton West , Rayleigh Bay , Edgemead and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Stepford Express services to Stepford Central , Newry Harbour , Rayleigh Bay and Llyn-by-the-Sea . It was added in Version 1.4 as part of the extension to Llyn-by-the-Sea , and overhauled in Version 2.0 . History [ ] 2019 17 December - Version 1.4 Westwyvern added to the network as part of the Llyn-by-the-Sea extension, as a major through station with 5 platforms, serving Stepford Connect and Stepford Express . Some services terminate early here at Platform 4. New routes: R024 , R025 , R026 , R077 & R078 2020 22 February - Version 1.4.1 Westwyvern is now managed by Stepford Express instead of Stepford Connect . Station upgraded with a rebuilt entrance, with the seating area removed. 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield branch . New routes: R035 , R036 , R037 & R038 29 October - Version 1.7 New routes: R080 & R082 2021 19 February - Version 1.7.2 Class 43 stop markers added to Platforms 2 & 3. New route: R040 5 December - Version 1.8 Added Stepford Connect services to Leighton West . Route changes: R037 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Llyn-by-the-Sea ) R038 ( Leighton Stepford Road ‚Üí Leighton City <> Westwyvern ) Now terminates at Leighton City. New route: R042 2023 17 July - Version 1.10.8 Class 80x stop markers added to Platforms 2 & 3. 2024 11 February Sneak peek for Westwyvern's overhaul released. Another day, another refurbished station üåá 12 August - Version 2.0 Station overhauled, now resembles more of Grantham station . A lounge and a station office has been added, located at Platform 1 and between Platform 2 & 4 respectively. Platforms decreased from 5 to 4. Platform 1 now also serves westbound Stepford Express services in addition to Stepford Connect . Platform 2 is now exclusive to eastbound Stepford Express services. Platform 3 is now the terminating platform. However, Platform 4 can still allow for terminating services. Platform 4 now serves as the eastbound platform for both Stepford Connect and Stepford Express . Added Stepford Connect & Stepford Express services to the Rayleigh Bay branch . New routes: R050 , R102 & R087 Trivia [ ] Westwyvern is based on Grantham station in Lincolnshire. This station, along with Millcastle , were the two stations on the Llyn-by-the-Sea extension that were not revealed on the SCR Official Discord server before opening. This is the first station to be managed by Stepford Express , with Leighton Stepford Road and Northshore following. All 3 stations were formerly managed by Stepford Connect . Strangely, the sign outside the station still showed Stepford Connect under the National Rail logo until V1.6 . From V1.4.1 to V1.6.5, although this station was managed by Stepford Express , dispatchers at this station were given the generic uniform (i.e. the uniform worn by dispatchers at stations managed by Network Rail ) despite the station not being operated by Network Rail . This was due to Stepford Express not having its own dispatching uniform at the time. This was eventually changed with the new uniforms in V1.7 . In V1.4.1 : The station signs on the platforms changed from Stepford Connect to Stepford Express , making Westwyvern the first station on the Network with Stepford Express station signs. Additionally, the entrance of this station was rebuilt and the seating area at the entrance has been removed. You could walk through the walls of the footbridge at this station, which was likely caused by developers forgetting to enable collision in Studio. This gets frustrating for players because they might fall onto the tracks and respawn. This was fixed in V1.7 . However, the walls of the elevators of the footbridge are still non-collidable. The approach ramp into the station was non-collidable, meaning it was possible to fall out of the ramp leading up to the footbridge into the station. When Faymere Green TMD was released, trains could now spawn there to Westwyvern instead of spawning all the way over at the now defunct Coxly Depot . Prior to V2.0 : This station had the least amount of scenery in the entire Llyn extension before its overhaul. There was a flyover to allow terminating trains to reach Platform 4. However, Stepford Connect trains headed to this station from Millcastle had a chance to be SPADed by Stepford Express trains on R082 ( Stepford Central <> Westwvyern ) as there was a crossover track for Stepford Express trains to go on the flyover, though this was quite rare as the Llyn Branch has less trains than the Stepford City or the Leighton Zone . As of V2.0 , this is still possible despite the switch to a tunnel. There is a very short platform on the opposite side of Platform 3, next to Platform 4. However, trains do not open their doors there because the platform is too short for most trains. In V1.7 , Stepford Express services can now terminate with R082 . This was the only station which provided cross-platform interchange between Stepford Connect and Stepford Express in both directions for trains travelling in the same direction. With the platform changes in V2.0 , this only applies to eastbound services. Passengers can, however, do a same-platform interchange at Platform 1. R081 , R083 , R085 and R088 skips this station despite it being owned by Stepford Express , making them the only routes in SCR able to skip this station. Routes that terminate at this station generally have poor timetables, causing on-time Drivers to have to wait multiple minutes at the terminating platform before being able to turn around or despawn. This station is the only station that has a station office, the interior consisting of two desks with computers and a CIS Board . Oddly, the sign at the office uses the old SCR logo. This is only available to players in the Dispatcher role or higher. The station office sign There is a church with a graveyard near the station that contains the tombstones of the removed Class 465 , Class 508 , Class 700 and Class 701 . ## Station 77: Whitefield

**Page ID:** 3225
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Whitefield

**Summary:**
Whitefield is the terminus of the Whitefield Branch . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley and Stepford Central .

**Full Content:**

Whitefield Main Entrance Side Entrance Parking Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Parked Class 170 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone WHF A Station headcode Dispatching F Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line No Whitefield Branch Station Information Location Whitefield District Zone - Platforms 3 Tracks 4 Accessibility Level access & step-free access via ramp Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Houghton Rake 0.8 mi / 1.3 km Woodhead Lane 1.3 mi / 2.1 km Terminus Whitefield is the terminus of the Whitefield Branch . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley and Stepford Central .
