History [ ] 2019 28 April - Version 1.2 Whitefield added to the network as part of the Whitefield extension as a Stepford Connect terminus. Based on Bradford Forster Square station. Only has a simple station building with no entrance. New routes: R020 & R022 17 December - Version 1.4 Station headcode: W ‚Üí F W was taken by Westwyvern . 2020 3 January Sneak peek for Whitefield's overhaul was released. Happy New Year from the SCR Team! We've been quiet since releasing V1.4 but I have been hard at work for you all! Coming soon to SCR: The Long awaited NG Class 465, NG Class 331 and a scenery upgrade for Whitefield, as well as a few other bits and bobs! üòÑ 22 February - Version 1.4.1 Station overhauled. Now has an entrance from a road outside. Platforms remain the same, but with Stepford Connect blue instead of Metro red. 2021 21 November Sneak peek for Whitefield's second overhaul was released. As has become a bit of a tradition... it is sneak peek Sunday! Here is another area and station upgrade, courtesy of @[SG] Mattyx2013. We hope you love it as much as we do! Coming soon to v1.8 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled. New station building and concourse with shops. Now based on Eastbourne station . Added a new spawn location Side Entrance . Island platform moved from Platform 1 & 2 to Platform 2 & 3. Added OHLE. Platform allocation is now randomised. Route change: R022 ( Stepford Victoria ‚Üí Beechley <> Whitefield ) Now terminates at Beechley. No longer stops at Stepford Victoria , Financial Quarter , City Hospital , Whitefield Lido & Houghton Rake . 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Platforms lowered to fix a issue with Mark 3 Coaches clipping through the platforms. Though this brought another issue where all station props (except benches) have disappeared. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 OHLE removed. Station props have been readded. New route: R103 Trivia [ ] When V1.2 released, Whitefield released with its original design from SCR Legacy , which was low quality, making it unappealing. The only recognisable differences were the implementations of CIS Boards and Concourse Information Boards , and the Stepford Connect signs. This station also lacked scenery compared to other stations on the branch, and on the network as a whole. It had no roads or paths, no buildings or scenery, and even lacked an entrance. The station received an entrance in this facelift. The station pillars were changed from " Metro red " to " Stepford Connect turquoise ." This station had a large "Welcome to Whitefield" sign outside, originally in Connect branding. A similar sign was also in place at Westercoast and Millcastle Racecourse . They were replaced by plain signs, and were eventually removed. Before the station was re-upgraded in V1.8 , many players stated that Whitefield looked similar to Connolly , a Waterline station. This is because of the platform arrangement and station design: Both stations had three platforms and were at the end of their respective branches. Both stations had a vintage-like brick colour. Both stations have platform canopies. Both stations have a train stabled there. Even though the station Whitefield Lido has the term "Whitefield" in its name, it is closer to Stepford Central than it is to Whitefield. This station is 3 stations apart from Whitefield Lido . This station has step-free access as the platforms are on ground level. Players can walk from here to Willowfield without trespassing or without going via another station. This station was well known for the boarded-up Metro commercial building adjacent to the station (this indicated that Metro was cancelled). However, in V1.8 , this was demolished with the second Whitefield upgrade. Before V1.8 , the station was sneak peeked with route indicators ; they did not come with V1.8 though. A preview with tracks curving to a terminating station, surrounded by scenery as well as a train wash on one of the tracks, was released on 22 November 2021, in the SCR Official Discord. This was eventually confirmed to be Whitefield on V1.8 's release. When players leave this station on a train, there is graffiti on the bridge that says " Matty Wuz 'Ere ": a nod to the fact that former Product Developer Mattyx2013 designed this station. The branch this station is located on ( Whitefield Branch ), along with the Leighton West Branch and the Rayleigh Bay Branch , are the only Stepford Connect branches to have no services to St Helens Bridge . This station is one of three stations to have a stabled train directly in it, the others being Connolly and Esterfield . This is the only station to have a stabled train that is not on Waterline . Between V2.0 and V2.2 , all of the light posts and station signs were accidentally removed while lowering the platforms to fix a clipping issue. A floating departure board on Platform 1 was fixed in V2.1 . Electric trains could previously serve this station until Version 2.2 , where the overhead line equipment was removed, only allowing diesel trains beyond Stepford UFC . Despite Whitefield still being a Stepford Connect station, Dispatchers now spawn with Metro uniforms. ## Station 78: Whitefield Lido

**Page ID:** 4835
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Whitefield_Lido

**Summary:**
Whitefield Lido is an elevated through station on the Whitefield Branch .

**Full Content:**

Whitefield Lido Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Whitefield Lido View 1 Whitefield Lido View 2 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone WFL A Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line Yes Whitefield Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Zone Stepford City Zone Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Stepford High Street 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Stepford United Football Club 0.6 mi / 1.0 km Track Layout To Stepford United Football Club To Stepford High Street Whitefield Lido is an elevated through station on the Whitefield Branch . It is served by Metro services to Willowfield , Stepford Victoria , Stepford Central and Stepford United Football Club . This station opened in Version 1.2 , and was overhauled in Version 1.8 . It was also part of the former Stepford City Zone . To play these files, consider using another device or convert them into supported formats such as .mp3. History [ ] 2019 17 February Sneak peek for Whitefield Lido was released. Hello! This is my first submission to the SCR Dev Team!! Everyone say hello to <top secret>. Coming soon to a SCR near you üòâ 28 April - Version 1.2 Whitefield Lido added to the network as part of the Whitefield extension , as a Stepford Connect through station with 3 platforms, with Platform 3 allowing for ECS trains from Whitefield Lido Siding . New routes: R020 , R021 , R022 & R023 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Added Stepford Connect services to the Willowfield Branch . New route: R031 2021 13 November Sneak peek for Whitefield Lido's overhaul was released. Sorry it has been a bit quiet on the sneak peek front! Unfortunately a lot of the team have been ill or away, but we've been continuing to work behind the scenes! So, here's yet another station refurb coming to you in v1.8, very soon! 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled. The station is now elevated. Now based on Wallasey Village station . Added OHLE and platform layout changed to side platforms. Scenery upgrade including a pool next to the station. Platform 3 removed along with Whitefield Lido Siding . Route removal: R022 No longer stops here. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Whitefield Lido is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect ; Stepford Connect no longer serves this station. Route removal: R020 No longer stops here. 5 August - Version 2.2 A poster named "A new chapter" was added next to the ticket machines. This won the first Community Spotlight hosted in May 2025. 'A new chapter' by martoto008 Trivia [ ] According to Mattyx2013, this station is based on the real life Wallasey Village station in Merseyside. There was formerly an advertisement on the billboard for West Benton Pet Supplies, which is located opposite West Benton station. This ad can now only be seen at Starryloch and Whitefield . Ironically, there is no West Benton Pet Supplies advertisement at West Benton station. This may be because it can be seen from the station. Despite this station being called "Whitefield Lido" (the word "lido" means a swimming pool or a beach), prior to Version 1.8 , there was no lido or body of water. There were only trees and a road near the entrance. The closest body of water would be the little water basin just underneath the approach to St Helens Bridge . Even though this station has the term "Whitefield" in its name, it is closer to Stepford Central than it is to Whitefield . This station is 3 stations apart, with a 3.11 mile (or 5.01 kilometres) distance from Whitefield . After V2.2 , there are no direct routes from here to Whitefield . There was once a pair of unused Tramlink platforms located under this station, but they were demolished when the station was released. Walking to Stepford United Football Club is possible by using the road running alongside the railway. Before Version 1.8 , trains exiting Whitefield Lido Siding would arrive on Platform 3. If Platform 2 was occupied, trains on the mainline could also use a crossover track to get to Platform 3, but this rarely happened as the Whitefield Branch was rarely busy. The siding was demolished in V1.8 , as well as the removal of Platform 3. For a while, the line was lifted north of here. This was likely because most of the stations were completely remodelled. Whitefield and Stepford High Street were the only stations that were not rebuilt. Stepford High Street was later rebuilt in V1.6 , but Whitefield and Whitefield Lido have remained basically the same. When the Whitefield Lido overhaul sneak peek for V1.8 showed only 2 platforms at the station, some feared that Whitefield Lido Siding would be demolished as part of the upgrade, which was confirmed when the update released. This station, along with Woodhead Lane and Faraday Road , are the few stations to have non-concrete platform bases. According to Mattyx2013 , he designed a new station model intended for Whitefield Lido at first, but the model was then changed to be used at James Street instead. [ 1 ] Eventually, the model was never used at either station. There is a rusty station sign that is near the entrance of the station, symbolising the former Stepford Connect operations. Oddly, when spawning here as a Dispatcher , the Stepford Connect uniform is given instead of a Metro one. Even stranger is that a Dispatcher will spawn with Metro uniform at Whitefield . This is likely to be a developer oversight. References [ ] ‚Üë Actual SCR Secrets (I Promise!) (29 September 2022). Mattyx2013 on YouTube. Notes [ ] ‚Üë This announcement was used in-game before the introduction of Metro , however, is no longer used. ## Station 79: Whitney Green

**Page ID:** 453
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Whitney_Green

**Summary:**
Whitney Green is a through station on the Greenslade Branch .

**Full Content:**

Whitney Green Spawn Entrance Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Tramlink Platforms Operational Information Served by Managed by (Not in service) [ in V2.3 ] (Not in service) [ in V2.3 ] Station code Signal zone WNG F Station headcode Dispatching - No Electrification Line Yes Greenslade Branch Station Information Location Morganstown District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via lifts Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Morganstown Docks 0.4 mi / 0.6 km Terminus (Not in service) Greenslade 0.9 mi / 1.5 km Robinson Way 0.4 mi / 0.6 km (Not in service) Preceding depot Following depot Whitney Green Depot - Whitney Green is a through station on the Greenslade Branch . It is served by Waterline services to Newry , Benton and Greenslade . There are 2 platforms for Tramlink services, but they are not in use. This station provides an out of station interchange (OSI) with the nearby Beaulieu Park served and operated by Metro . This station will be receiving an upgrade in Version 2.3 , with Metro serving and co-managing the station. It is also speculated that the Tramlink platforms will be removed. History [ ] 2017 16 December Whitney Green added to the network, as a Waterline through station with 2 platforms; and a Tramlink terminus. Announcement change: The Waterline announcement is now: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:WGW.ogg instead of: https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/File:WGC.ogg 2025 5 November Sneak peek for Whitney Green's upgrade was released. A green light has been given to a slightly red makeover. üü¢üîµüî¥ Coming to SCR version 2.3 Trivia [ ] Whitney Green has remained almost the exact same since it was first opened before V1.0 . The only changes have been the addition of lifts and new scenery. As such, it is currently the oldest station in-game, in terms of when it was last updated, having never received any major upgrade. When Version 2.3 releases, this will no longer be the case. This station has the shortest platforms in the whole SCR network. This station and Morganstown Docks , are the only stations on the SCR network where the platforms are only long enough for 3 coaches (with the exception of the double Class 143 ). When a 4-car train approaches this station, the onboard announcement will state that the doors in the rear coach will not open. When driving a 3-car Class 195 , the driver will be prompted to move forward when the driver stopped at the S Car Marker perfectly. This also applies to Morganstown Docks. Players can walk to Beaulieu Park on Metro from this station, which means that these two stations are out of station interchanges between Metro and Waterline and is one of the three out of station interchanges in SCR. The other two are between Airport West and Stepford Airport Parkway , as well as between Coxly and Coxly Newtown . Strangely, the Tramlink tracks have been electrified along with Waterline in V1.4.1 . This is a reason why numerous users believe Tramlink is coming back. However, in V1.7.0 , the tracks here have been covered by a mesh, like in Port Benton . This did not apply to Robinson Way and Greenslade . Tramlink tracks here have also had some grass/weeds placed on them in Version 1.7 , possibly to signify that Tramlink is long gone and will not return. The grass on the Tramlink tracks Oddly, in V1.8 , the grass on the tracks were removed, causing confusion. Oddly, the stairs at the station entrance next to the ramp are floating as the stair does not touch the ground. The lifts walls at this station do not fully line up as well. This station is believed to be named after BanTech's real name, Adam Whitney, shown in the registration information of his company website . This station's name used to be censored in game chat. In order to get around this, players called Whitney Green by its acronym: WG , or bypassed the filter by typing Whit ney Green . Some users believe that the Roblox chat filter censors Whitney Green because the phrase "ney green" may be mistakenly identified as containing a racial slur. ## Station 80: Willowfield

**Page ID:** 13393
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Willowfield

**Summary:**
Willowfield is a terminus on the Willowfield Branch . It provides Stepford Connect services to Whitefield , Port Benton , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Metro services to Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily and Barton .

**Full Content:**

Willowfield Entrance Interior Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Bird's Eye View Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone WFD A Station headcode Dispatching D Yes (1 slot) P1-3 Electrification Line Yes Willowfield Branch Station Information Location Stepford District Zone - Platforms 3 Tracks 3 Accessibility Level access Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Ticket gates Service Information Preceding station Following station Terminus Hemdon Park 1.22 miles / 1.96 kilometres Beechley 2.74 miles / 4.41 kilometres Preceding depot Following depot - Willowfield Station Depot Track Layout Willowfield Depot to Hemdon Park Willowfield is a terminus on the Willowfield Branch . It provides Stepford Connect services to Whitefield , Port Benton , Westwyvern and Llyn-by-the-Sea ; and Metro services to Stepford Victoria , Stepford United Football Club , Berrily and Barton . Opened in Version 1.6 , Willowfield station serves the small town of Willowfield. It features 3 bay platforms under a partially glazed canopy roof. Situated next to EKIA, it is known for Stepford's first-ever standalone clock and dedicated waiting shelter. This station has been step-free since Version 1.6. History [ ] 2020 22 June - Version 1.6 Willowfield added to the network as part of the Willowfield extension , as a Stepford Connect terminus with 3 platforms. New routes: R028 , R030 , R031 , R032 , R035 & R036 Bug : Buffers do not despawn trains. 23 June Bugfix : Buffers now despawn trains properly. 1 January - Version 1.7.1 Bug : Doors open on the wrong side. Depot ‚Üí WIL P1, then P2, then P3 Mainline ‚Üí WIL P3, then P2, then P1 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 Willowfield is now managed by Metro instead of Stepford Connect . New routes: R103 & R133 Trivia [ ] This is the westernmost station in SCR. The name "Willowfield" was the original name for Financial Quarter in Metro 's original network plans. Before V1.0 , Willowfield only existed on a map. There was no station model. Unlike Beechley and City Hospital , which were only separated by around 600 metres, Willowfield is nowhere near Financial Quarter , as it is around 6 kilometres away. This station and Hemdon Park were not previewed before the release of the Willowfield Branch . Before V1.6.1, trains were able to drive through the buffers as they were non-collidable. However, this was patched the following day. The longest route on any operator starts here, being R036 ( Willowfield <> Llyn-by-the-Sea ). This route is exclusive to the Class 68 and Class 444 . This station, Morganstown , and Westercoast have the longest single-word station names. The longest overall is Stepford United Football Club . Willowfield Depot is just south of this station. Only trains from the station depot will arrive at Willowfield, and trains from the mainline depot directly go to Hemdon Park or Beechley . Players can walk from here to Whitefield without trespassing or without going via any other station. This is one of two stations where its depot leads straight to the station, with all routes terminating there. The other station with this trait is Esterfield . Edgemead Siding used to have this trait, until it was removed as part of the Edgemead upgrade in V1.7.2. Dispatcher trainings were held here from V1.7.4. Previously, they were held at Stepford United Football Club . Trainings were later moved back to Stepford United Football Club in V1.8 , before being moved to a separate training map. This station only has one bench and one waiting house on its platforms, making it the station with the lowest amount of benches. Oddly, players can walk on the track beds behind the buffers without being despawned. Taken prior to the opening of Willowfield Depot . ## Station 81: Winstree

**Page ID:** 14807
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Winstree

**Summary:**
Removed feature

**Full Content:**

Removed feature This article or section is about content, which has once been in the game, but was later completely removed from the game. They are considered as removed features. Removed feature This article or section is about content, which has once been in the game, but was later completely removed from the game. They are considered as removed features. Winstree The since-demolished Winstree station, a few months before being replaced. Operational Information Served by Managed by High Speed Station code WIN Station Information Zone Leighton Zone Platforms 6 (4 were used) Tracks 6 (5 attached to platforms) Accessibility Step-free access was available Service Information Preceding station Following station Water Newton Terminus Leighton [ note 1 ] Preceding depot Following depot Benton Depot Winstree Depot Winstree is a demolished station that was in use between 29th November 2017 and 21st April 2018 until it was demolished and replaced by Leighton Stepford Road in The Big Update . It was served by Connect services to Stepford Town . This station is infamous for being the only demolished station in the history of the entire network. Prior to The Big Update, it garnered a wave of sympathy, with staff even organising farewell events. It is speculated that Winstree was removed as former SCR Developer Jadey_SR requested its removal after Managing Director Charlie_RBX shared plans of continuing SCR for profit. Around the same time, former SCR Developer vOranges uncopylocked the game, which was another contributory factor, and it resulted in the release of multiple unofficial 'SCR Legacy' games. Just before the removal, many players gathered around the station, organising farewell events to say goodbye to Winstree for good. The site of the station now is the BanTech Systems building, opposite Rocket Parade . Contents 1 Former Track & Platform Layout 2 Trivia 3 Notes 4 Gallery Former Track & Platform Layout [ ] -] Terminus << Passing Service Direction == Unused Track Platforms/Tracks Services/Use 1 Terminating, Connect services to Stepford Town -] -] 2 3 Not in use ==] 4 == << Connect services from Winstree Depot to Stepford Town 5 6 << Trivia [ ] Some of the platforms had a sign with a 'HS' logo signifying an old, abandoned project called HighSpeed . Platform 6 was originally also intended to be for services terminating from Llyn-by-the-Sea , but due to the removal of Winstree, this never happened. This station was designed based on Colchester , a station on the Greater Anglia network in Essex, UK. Notes [ ] ‚Üë Prior to Winstree's removal, the tracks beyond the station ran to Winstree Depot and an unopened station called "Leighton" (which is widely believed to be an old version of the station now known as Leighton City ). However, there were no services that went there, making it inaccessible by all means except through trespassing . Gallery [ ] The HS (HighSpeed) signs at Winstree. Dispatchers holding up their batons in solidarity of the loss of Winstree, as passengers watch. The last ever trains at Winstree. ## Station 82: Woodhead Lane

**Page ID:** 2872
**URL:** https://scr.fandom.com/wiki/Woodhead_Lane

**Summary:**
Woodhead Lane is a through station located along the Whitefield Branch .

**Full Content:**

Woodhead Lane Spawn Platform View 1 Platform View 2 Platform View 3 Operational Information Served by Managed by Station code Signal zone WHL A Station headcode Dispatching - Yes (1 slot) P1-2 Electrification Line No Whitefield Branch Station Information Location Whitefield District Zone - Platforms 2 Tracks 2 Accessibility Step-free access via ramps Ticket machines Yes Ticketing Card reader Service Information Preceding station Following station Stepford United Football Club 1.2 mi / 1.9 km Houghton Rake 0.5 mi / 0.8 km Whitefield 1.3 mi / 2.1 km Track Layout to Houghton Rake Woodhead Lane to Woodhead Lane TMD Woodhead Lane is a through station located along the Whitefield Branch . It is served by Stepford Connect services to Willowfield , Beechley , Stepford Central and Whitefield . This station was first released in Version 1.2 on 28 April 2019, and received an overhaul as part of Version 1.8 on 5 December 2021. Build number 4 and I think that I can safely say that this is the most scenic station so far üòÅ 28 April - Version 1.2 Woodhead Lane added to the network as part of the Whitefield extension , as a Stepford Connect through station with 2 side platforms. Resembles Southease station . A brown footbridge in the station connects the platforms. New routes: R020 & R022 2021 11 September Sneak peek for Woodhead Lane's overhaul was released. üåá Thanks to some help from ex-developer, @[SG] Mattyx2013 , who's done some one-off work for us - here's an area that needed some love, but where is it? ü§î Also here's the first one of many upgraded scenery features on trial here thanks to @[PDV] MrTransportGuy - what do we all think?! Coming to an v1.8 near you! 5 December - Version 1.8 Station overhauled. No longer resembles Southease station . Platform layout changed from side platforms to staggered platforms, footbridge removed. Added OHLE and Stop Markers for the Class 720 and Class 730/1 . Route change: R022 ( Stepford Victoria ‚Üí Beechley <> Whitefield ) Now terminates at Beechley. No longer stops: Stepford Victoria , Financial Quarter , City Hospital , Whitefield Lido & Houghton Rake 2024 12 August - Version 2.0 Platforms have been lowered and extended slightly to fit certain trains better. 2025 11 May - Version 2.2 OHLE removed. New route: R103 Trivia [ ] This station formerly resembled Southease station in real life prior to its overhaul. The rail crossing , as with the other gates in-game (notably Houghton Rake and Westercoast ), are not functional. They are set to the "down" position, even if no trains are scheduled. This station has step-free access. Fully working rail crossings can be found on the former SCR roadmap, but they are not in earnest priority according to former Managing Director Charlie_RBX . During a developer Q&A on 23 October 2021, he stated, "[they] will not come in the short term as [they are] not on the top of the priority list." It is also unknown if signals for pedestrians and road traffic will be implemented. The original station was revealed on 16 March 2019, by former Product Developer Mattyx2013 . This station is within walking distance of Stepford United Football Club and Whitefield Lido . "Woodhead" is the surname of the former Managing Director Charlie_RBX in real life. In a Q&A, it was revealed that the station was named after him. This is the only in-game reference to former Managing Director Charlie_RBX after the controversy in 2022. This station, as well as Whitefield Lido , are the only stations to have poles holding the platforms up instead of traditional concrete blocks. All stations had this feature introduced after their upgrades. This station and Aslockby are the only stations to feature staggered side platforms. Between V1.8 and V1.9.1, Ashlan Park also shared this trait, until staggered platforms were removed when the station received an upgrade in V1.9.1. If the player walks to the end of the road, they can travel under the station. Under the baseplate, there used to be an old bridge that used to stretch towards Houghton Rake . This is technically a glitch, as this is not supposed to happen. Therefore, this can also be considered trespassing . This bridge was in use up until V1.8 , where the alignment of the Whitefield Branch changed to feature more curves, bringing it to the standards of SCR's more recent output. Woodhead Lane was one of the stations used to train Dispatchers between its original release and Version 1.4 , when trainings were moved to the vicinity of Faymere . Trainings returned to the station shortly after Version 1.6.5 released, continuing until a new map was created for training. The platforms at this station are not long enough for trains with 5 cars or more. There are special purple stop markers for the Class 720 and 730 here to allow them to fit better on the platforms. These special stop markers were removed in Version 2.2 due to the line beyond Stepford UFC becoming diesel only. Now, the only train that doesn't fully fit is the Class 68 where the rear locomotive car does not fit on the platform. Oddly enough, this station has no ticket machines.
